(6) 150 square li | 9,000 tons | Same as above | 24 zhang | Same as above | Due south | 42 li | Hongchang | Daily output about 8 tons

(7) 90 square li | 540 tons | Same as above | 24 zhang | Same as above | Due east | 32 li | Sijingke | Daily output about 8 tons

(8) 140 li | 8,400 tons | Same as above | 24 zhang | Same as above | Same as above | Due east | 33 li | Zhongjingke | Daily output about 13 tons

The above eight mines have all been mined, but mines 5, 6, and 8 have been stopped. In addition, there are smaller mines such as Yongshou Village, Xicun, Zhongquan, Liangshui Spring, Yushi Ao, and Shangdian, which have also been mined.

▲ Ash Dump Coal Mine. On the afternoon of the 18th, on the way to Tongguan, we took the opportunity to inspect the Ash Dump Coal Mine, which is about 5 li from Tongguan County. There are two wells open, both 180 feet deep. The two wells are 25 feet apart, and the coal seam has three layers. The first layer is 2 feet thick, the second layer is 5 feet thick, and the third layer is 2 feet 5 inches. The first and second layers are 12 feet apart, and the second and third layers are 5 feet apart. The well was opened in the 26th year of Guangxu in the late Qing Dynasty. The diameter is about 16 feet, and it is 10 feet from the ground, built with brick and stone. The remaining 6 feet are left to nature. The coal seam runs north-south, sloping east or west about 10 degrees (coal seam inclined). Each large shift has 22 workers, including 12 coal miners, 14 or 15 coal pullers, and 4 or 5 casual workers (no fixed job). Each day, they need to produce about 800 to 900 baskets of coal (150 jin per basket). The second coal seam is currently being mined. The wages for each person in the well for each large shift are 17 yuan. The wages for the 8 people who operate the winch above the well are 2 yuan and 4 jiao for every 50 baskets. The hemp rope for the winch is 5 minutes in diameter, and each rope is 5 feet long, weighing about 1 jin and costing 4 jiao. The hemp rope must be replaced once every 40 days. The miners go up and down, and two people can stand in each basket. The coal is loaded into a rectangular basket in the well, which is 18 inches long, 8 inches wide, and 5 inches high, and can hold 40 jin of coal. The lifting is done with a round large basket, 15 inches in diameter and 15 inches deep. The coal has smoke. Local kilns have been opened within 20 li east of Huikan. The height and width of the coal lanes in the well are each 5 feet. Because the roof is hard, no supports are used. The coal is mined using the room and pillar method, and the coal pillars are 12 feet square. The annual coal production is about 20,000 to 30,000 baskets, totaling more than 2,000 tons. Work starts for 10 months each year, with 10 to 60 workers. 30 yuan are paid to the merchants each month, and 30 yuan are paid as coal tax. In addition, 10 baskets of coal are paid to the county government for each large shift. The selling price of raw coal is 5 jiao per basket, and the price of lump coal is 5 jiao per 100 jin. The burning fire method is commonly used in the mine. For this system, another inclined well is opened 100 feet below the air outlet well, and a fire is burned at the bottom of the inclined well, and the surface of the air outlet well is covered and blocked. The hot air rises from the inclined well, and the cold air enters the well from the air inlet well, so that the workers underground can work without suffocating.

▲ Baigong Temple Coal Mine. At half past seven on the morning of the 19th, we took more than a dozen donkeys to Baigong Temple to investigate the coal mine. The journey took about 10 hours, and we returned at about 6 pm. The road was full of high mountains and steep slopes. Sometimes, because the slope was too steep, we had to get off the donkeys and crawl up, which was very laborious. The results are as follows: The mine is located 25 li southeast of the county seat and was opened in the 11th year of the Republic of China. There are two vertical wells, arranged east and west, 20 feet apart, and each 6 feet in diameter and 110 feet deep. 1,500 to 1,600 yuan of capital has been used. The first layer has been reached, the coal is 6 feet thick, sloping northwest, and running northeast-southwest. There are 15 people in the well, including one foreman, six coal miners, seven coal pullers, and one casual worker. Each large shift is 7 days, and each person's wages for each large shift are 5 yuan, and a total of more than 50 baskets of coal must be produced. The wages for the 6 people who operate the winch above the well and the 2 people who send the coal to the pile are 5 jiao per day. 120 baskets can be hoisted per day. There is currently more than 1 zhang of accumulated water in the well, part of which is water from abandoned wells and part of which is surface water. At present, the water is being pumped out with cowhide bags, which can hold 100 jin of water per bag. Two people can pump out 100 bags of water in 12 hours. Each support in the well uses three pieces of wood, the beam is 3 feet long, the legs are 4 feet long, and the wood is 6 inches in diameter. The price of each support is 9 jiao. The wood used for the horizontal support on the two wood supports is 6 feet long and 2 inches in diameter, and each piece of wood costs about 1 jiao. The mine pays 100 yuan to the merchants each quarter, 40 yuan per month for coal tax, and 2 yuan for special tax. The selling price of coal is about 4 to 5 baskets per yuan. (To be continued)

Soviet Government Rejects Puppet State's Protest 60

Declares That Russian Troops Did Not Invade Manchurian Territory

Also States That No Defensive Works Were Built in Manchuli

▲Tass News Agency, Moscow, 28th - Soviet Consul-General in Harbin, Slavutsky, delivered to the Foreign Affairs Commissioner of Jilin Province a document from the Soviet government in response to the protest from the Jilin authorities. At the same time, it declared that the situation in Manchuli on the border has remained unchanged for many years, and no disputes have occurred.

Puppet State Mail Accepted in the U.S. as Usual 61

In Accordance with Procedures for Russian Mail

But Does Not Constitute Recognition of Puppet State Stamps

▲Kokumin News Agency, Washington, 27th - Regarding the issue of international mail from the Manchukuo puppet state, U.S. postal authorities recently told a representative of the Kokumin News Agency that since the Manchukuo post office was separated from Chinese jurisdiction, the U.S. side has temporarily accepted mail coming to the U.S. with "Manchukuo puppet state" stamps in accordance with the procedures for handling Soviet Russian mail because the so-called "Manchukuo puppet state's" international status has not yet been determined. However, this does not constitute recognition of the "Manchukuo puppet state" stamps, and this is not a final decision, as it is still necessary to consult with various countries in the Universal Postal Union on how to handle it. According to U.S. postal authorities, this postal issue may cause disputes. The U.S. government has decided to refuse recognition of Manchukuo, as can be seen from the State Department's repeated statements since Japan's invasion of Manchuria.

Content of Japanese Immigration Plan to Northeast China 63

Budgeted Expenses 208,000 Yen

With Veterans as the Mainstay of Immigration

▲The World News Agency says that the Japanese Kwantung Army Special Service Department and the Shenyang branch office director of the Colonization Ministry, Secretary Nagai, have recently conducted detailed research on agricultural immigration to Manchuria, both theoretically and practically, and have created a concrete plan. Lieutenant Colonel Yokoyama of the Special Service Department has brought it back to Tokyo to discuss it further with the relevant authorities of the Colonization Ministry, so as to create a definite immigration plan, and immigration matters will be carried out according to the plan thereafter. The estimated expenses are 208,000 yen, and it has been decided to submit it to the Provisional Parliament. The contents of the concrete plan created by Nagai are recorded as follows: (1) The immigration site is located in the two areas of the Ba Hulicao River tributary, 12 li south of Sanxing Guimusi in Jilin Province (with approximately 270,000 Qing of uncultivated agricultural land). (2) Immigrants may not bring family members, and 500 men will be recruited first. (3) The 500 immigrants will be composed of 100 students from the Xideng Elementary School, which is currently training in agricultural affairs at the Beida Camp in Shenyang, 100 people who will be sent to the school from Japan, and 300 others. The other 300 people will be composed of agricultural immigrants who have already arrived in Manchuria and local farmers. (4) The immigration method will adopt the Tuntian soldier system, with veterans as the main component. (5) The immigration business will focus on farming and animal husbandry, with paddy fields only being a part of it. After the immigration plan expenses are approved by the Provisional Parliament, recruitment of immigrants will begin and they will be sent to the Eastern Provinces.

Japanese Seiyukai Softens Toward Government 65

Frontal Conflict Between Both Sides in Parliament Can Be Avoided

Minister of Justice Reports Truth of May 15th Incident

▲Dentsu News Agency, Tokyo, 28th - The two issues of the Rice Law Amendment Bill and the Debt Consolidation Association Law are sufficient to brew a crisis of frontal conflict between the government and the Seiyukai. However, the government anticipates that it can reach a compromise with the Seiyukai. The Seiyukai executives still maintain (1) that in addition to removing the tax-rate-based rice price in the Rice Law Amendment issue, colonial rice must be purchased and disaster relief rice must be delivered free of charge, (2) that the Central Treasury Law for responsible consolidation associations must be passed, still adhering to the party's position. Later, the government expressed its approval for removing the tax-rate-based rice price, and the hardline opinions within the Seiyukai greatly eased as a result, and they still intend to proceed with parliamentary business, with the intention of attaching a resolution of hope to the government's original proposal and approving it. Since the attitude of the majority party, the Seiyukai, has softened, the Provisional Parliament will likely not experience turbulence.

▲Dentsu News Agency, Tokyo, 28th - Yesterday, Minister of Justice Oyama reported the truth of the May 15th Incident in a closed session of the House of Representatives as follows: The Minister of Justice first explained the situation of the Blood Oath Corps, and then turned to the May 15th Incident, saying that the assassination of Junnosuke Inoue and Takuma Dan continued to occur this spring. Fourteen people were prosecuted for their relationship with the Blood Oath Corps, with Nissho Inoue as the center. Among them were eight students from the Imperial University, Kyoto University, and Kokugakuin University. These people, indignant at the current situation, planned to assassinate ten political figures and ten business leaders. The plan was suspended because the Inoue assassination was discovered and they were subsequently arrested. Those who were indignant and rose up in succession were the members of the Aikyo School, proceeding with the same purpose. Twelve members of the faction and four related persons, with 00 as the leader, first contacted everything at the Koga Town in Ibaraki Prefecture through naval officers and technical school students among the comrades. In addition to the twelve naval officers involved, there was one reserve officer, ten military academy students, and one dropout. Before the implementation, 00 met with a certain person at his home on April 3rd, giving him a pistol and 140 rounds of ammunition. Thereafter, up to May 13th, 00 handed over 6,000 yen to a certain person several times. On the day of the implementation, they were divided into three groups. The first group gathered at the Shokonsha Shrine to attack the Prime Minister's residence, the second group gathered at Sengakuji Temple to attack the residence of Makino Naifu, and the third group gathered at Shinbashi Station to attack the Seiyukai headquarters. These three groups all planned to attack the Metropolitan Police Department at 1:30 PM. A certain person from another faction attacked the Bank of Japan, a certain person attacked Mitsubishi Bank, and a certain person planned to kill Seida, who tried to stop this plan. The Minister of Justice ended his explanation here, and there were no questions, and then the meeting adjourned.

Revolution in the South American Republic of Ecuador 66

Revolutionary Army Controls the Capital and Threatens Parliament

Acting President Flees to the Argentine Embassy

▲Kokumin News Agency, Guayaquil (Ecuador), 27th - News received today that Bonifaz, the elected president whose qualifications were rejected by the Ecuadorian Congress, has launched an uprising in the capital and occupied the public mansion. Acting President Moreno has fled to the U.S. Embassy. Bonifaz was elected president on October 20, 1931, for a five-year term, but because his parents were Peruvian, the Congress decided that his qualifications were not met and he was unable to take office. Subsequent news reported that the incident developed so rapidly that it has clearly become a national revolution. Acting President Moreno has changed his refuge to the Argentine Embassy. German Government Attempts to Vigorously Complete Economic Reform Plan 67

Compromise Reached with Center Party

New Parliament Unlikely to Be Dissolved Immediately

▲Kokumin News Agency, Berlin, 27th - The German government is currently concentrating all its efforts on completing its economic reform plan. Its manifesto was completed tonight after revisions. According to financial sources, the government no longer employs the method of forcefully issuing public bonds, but still insists on levying an industrial tax, which is inevitable, but will not affect the working capital of industry and agriculture.

▲Reuter's, Berlin, 27th - It is rumored that the Center Party and the Nazi Party have reached a compromise after lengthy negotiations. If this rumor is true, there will be a fundamental change in Germany's political future. There will be a mixed party occupying the majority in Parliament, and a parliamentary government will continue to exist because there will no longer be a reason to dissolve Parliament. According to public speculation, the new cabinet will have Nazi leader Strasser as Prime Minister, Brunner of the Center Party as Foreign Minister, and Schleicher as Minister of Defense.

▲Kokumin News Agency, Berlin, 27th - If the German Parliament is dissolved within a week of its convocation, whether Chancellor von Papen will follow the constitution and hold a re-election within sixty days, or temporarily postpone the election by implementing essential policies by presidential emergency decree, remains a major question lingering in the minds of Germans at this time. Today, the Korolyev Daily commented, claiming to have received reliable information that the government, in view of the current political turmoil and the fact that the German people have experienced several election campaigns in recent months, such as two presidential elections and several state parliament and national parliament elections, if the entire country is immediately thrown into the turmoil of electoral competition again, there is a danger that may occur. Therefore, if the Parliament is dissolved, it seems that the election should be temporarily postponed for the welfare of the country, and all forces should be concentrated on dealing with economic difficulties and safely overcoming the winter. If everything goes well, it is hoped that an election can be held according to the new election law next spring. The newspaper commented on this plan, believing that Chancellor von Papen apparently no longer counts on the possibility of cooperation between the Nazi Party and the Center Party, but if this cooperation can be realized, it is expected that the president and the chancellor will not insist on dissolving the Parliament either.

Japanese Steal Marine Products in Southwest China 71

▲Japanese Fishing Boats Catch Fish in Shanwei

▲Our Marine Product Boat Robbed Near Dongsha Island

Guangzhou Correspondence, Recently, the Japanese not only invade our Northeast step by step, but also send warships to plunder our marine products on the sea. Near the southwest coast, there have recently been two incidents of marine products being plundered. The reason is that several Japanese fishing boats have been arbitrarily catching fresh fish in the Shanwei sea area, and using electric boats to transport fish to and from various ports. Even Japanese fishing boats have broken into the outer harbor of Mayu Port in Shantou, stealing fish and transporting the captured fish to Hong Kong, changing trademarks, posing as foreign fish, and re-selling them in Shantou and the Nanyang area. This is one thing. Secondly, Dongsha Island has always had a Chinese fishing company, but the fishing boats it sent out were forcibly robbed by Japanese ships, resulting in the destruction of the company's Dongmei electric boat and the killing of five crew members. Manager Feng of the company has reported the theft of marine products by Japanese ships on Dongsha Island, the destruction of our fishing boats, and the killing of our crew members to the Guangdong Construction Department and forwarded to the Guangzhou Municipal Government to negotiate with the Japanese consulate. The Japanese consulate replied, falsely claiming that there was no evidence and ignoring it. However, at the beginning of this case, it was reported by the Dongsha Island Radio Station, and a commissioner was assigned by the Construction Department to take detailed statements from the four injured crew members Zhou Chu and others, and the Dongsha Island Director Li was approved by telegram to re-investigate clearly, and the evidence was conclusive. Recently, marine product company merchants have re-calculated the marine product losses for this year according to the budgeted amount of investment and reference to the selling price, and the value of the loss of electric boat guns and bullets, as well as the number of families of the five crew members who died requiring compensation, and have submitted a detailed document to the Construction Department, along with the case, to the Guangzhou Municipal Government, to negotiate with the Japanese Consul in Guangzhou again to achieve full compensation in order to make up for the losses and protect territorial sovereignty. The company's request for compensation from the Japanese Consul is as follows: (1) The annual production of sea-man grass is about 2,500 dan (according to 100 jin per dan), with each dan worth about 40 yuan at the time, the loss is 100,000 yuan; (1) The annual production of shellfish is about 500 dan, with each dan worth 30 yuan at the time, the total loss is 15,000 yuan; (1) Destruction of one Dongmei electric boat, loss of 9,000 yuan; (1) Four self-defense rifles were plundered, loss of 560 yuan; (1) 300 bullets were plundered, loss of 45 yuan; (1) The families of the five crew members who were killed requested 5,000 yuan in compensation each, totaling 25,000 yuan. The total compensation required is 149,605 yuan. After the authorities received the report, the Municipal Government has negotiated with the Japanese Consul again. (August 25th)

Shantou Business Community Still Opposes Business Tax 72

▲Business Tax Bureau Extends Implementation Period Again

Shantou Correspondence, The Shantou business community opposed the business tax, and a committee was organized by 52 businesses to request a postponement, and Wu Sihai and four others were sent to the province to petition and investigate the actual situation of the business tax implementation in various places for reference. Therefore, this case has not yet been resolved. The opinions held by the business community against the business tax are (1) that there are many special taxes and miscellaneous levies after the abolition of Likin, and the burden on the people is even greater than before Likin; (2) that the import and export tax rates of the customs have increased, and the government has defense, road construction, aviation volunteer bonds, civil aviation and other bonds, which amount to thousands of millions at every turn, burdening the people; (3) that the business tax rate is heavier than anywhere else, and the procedures are difficult and complicated, and it is difficult for merchants to do it. Director Hu Guannan of the Business Tax Bureau also knows the opinions of the merchants, but he cannot change the regulations without authorization. If it is handled too hastily, it may cause a strike. The first extension was for ten days, which expired on the 18th. Very few businesses complied. The bureau had no choice but to issue another notice extending it for ten days, declaring that there would be no further extensions and announcing the tax rates for various industries as follows, calculated on the capital amount: (1) Printing and publishing industry, (2) Goods sales industry, (3) Savings industry, (4) Barber industry, 5 per thousand for each of the above; (5) Manufacturing and processing industry (6) Banking industry (7) Transportation industry, 10 per thousand for each of the above; (8) Silver shop industry 15 per thousand; (10) Telephone industry, electricity industry, 2 per thousand. Sales tax amount, (1) Real estate industry, (2) Trust industry, 10 per thousand for each of the above; (3) Bath industry, (4) Goods leasing industry, (5) Tea house industry, 15 per thousand for each of the above; (6) Photography industry, 20 per thousand. Business tax amount, (1) Food and beverage sales industry, (2) Hotel industry, 2 per thousand for each of the above; (3) Hotel industry, 50 per thousand; (4) Western clothing industry, 3 per thousand. Income amount, (1) Contract engineering industry 3 per thousand (2) Railway industry 20 per thousand (3) Warehouse industry 10 per thousand (4) Wharf industry, (5) Market industry, (6) Slaughter industry, (7) Advertising industry 30 per thousand for each of the above; (8) Entertainment venue industry, 40 per thousand. Remuneration amount, (1) Bank industry 40 per thousand (2) Tax reporting industry 30 per thousand (4) Agency industry 50 per thousand (5) Brokerage industry in various industries 50 per thousand (August 19th)

Shanxi Plague Spreads Rampantly 73

▲Yongji, Yishi, Linjin and Other Counties Are the Most Severe

▲Residents of the Provincial Capital Are Also Panic-Stricken

Taiyuan Correspondence, The plague in Shanxi Province has been getting worse in recent days. Almost all of the 36 counties in the Hedong area of southern Shanxi have been affected. According to telegrams received by the Provincial Epidemic Prevention Office from various counties, Yongji, Yishi, and Linjin are the most tragic. More than 2,000 people have died in Linjin, and more than 1,000 people have died in Yongji and Yishi. More than 4,000 people have died in these three counties alone. In the remaining Xinxing, Wenxi, Quwo, Yuncheng, Anyi, Jiexi and other places, there are also deaths every day. Although the bus between Yuncheng and Fenglingdu has been suspended, Yuncheng has tightly closed the city gates and implemented inspections, and actively defended together with the medical committee members sent by the Provincial Epidemic Prevention Office, but the epidemic is still fierce and difficult to eradicate for a while. Originally, only Datong and Hequ in northern Shanxi discovered the plague, but recently Daixian, Pinglu and other places have also had the plague, with about 20 to 30 deaths per day. Daixian is only 300 to 400 li away from the province, so the residents of the provincial capital are all panic-stricken, and almost everyone is afraid that a natural disaster is about to strike. (22nd)

Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway and Joint Transportation of Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railways 74

▲ Beginning October 1st of this year

Hangzhou Communication: Since the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway opened to traffic from Hangzhou to Lanxi, its business has gradually developed. The Construction Department is now actively raising funds to build the Yushan section within Jiangxi Province, to facilitate military affairs and freight transportation, and is purchasing a large number of vehicles to be assembled and put into use at the factory. In order to facilitate the travel of passengers from Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo, a joint transportation contract has been signed with the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railways. The contract has been formally signed, and the railway bureaus of both parties have submitted it to the Ministry of Railways and the Construction Department for review and filing. It has been agreed that joint transportation will be implemented from October 1st of this year. The original text of the contract is recorded as follows: The Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Administration (hereinafter referred to as Party A) and the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway Engineering Bureau (hereinafter referred to as Party B) have entered into a contract with the following clauses for handling joint transportation matters: (1) The procedures for joint transportation matters, the format, and the responsibilities shared by Party A and Party B shall be handled in accordance with the domestic joint transportation regulations. For matters not stipulated in the domestic joint transportation regulations due to special circumstances, Party A and Party B may negotiate and determine them, but only to the extent that they do not violate the principles of the domestic joint transportation regulations. (2) Joint transportation revenue shall be settled once a month, and shall be handled by Party A and Party B in accordance with domestic joint transportation regulations. (3) Joint transportation stations: Party A includes Nanjing, Zhenjiang, Changzhou, Wuxi, Suzhou, Shanghai North Station, Shanghai South Station, Songjiang, Jiaxing, Xiashi, Chang'an, and Gongchenqiao, eleven stations in total. Party B includes Zhufeng, Paitou, Anhua, Suxi, Yiwu, Jinhua, and Lanxi, seven stations in total. (4) The connecting station for Party A is Nanxingqiao Station, and the connecting ticket office for Party B is Sanlangmiao. (5) The scope of joint transportation business is temporarily limited to three types: "one-way" passenger tickets, luggage, and packages. The types of passenger cars are first-class, second-class, and third-class, and four types of joint transportation passenger tickets that combines fourth-class for Party A's Shanghai North Station, Shanghai South Station, Songjiang, Jiaxing, Xiashi, and Chang'an, six stations in total, for departures and arrivals at each of these stations, and third-class for Party B. (6) Joint transportation passengers should be guided by Party A's Shangxingqiao Station to Party B's Sanlangmiao ticket office, where they will be taken care of to cross the river. (7) Luggage and packages transported by Party A to Party B shall be transported by Party A's Nanxingqiao Station to Party B's Sanlangmiao ticket office. Those transported by Party B to Party A shall be sent by Party B's Sanlangmiao ticket office to Party A's Nanxingqiao Station. (8) This contract shall be made in duplicate, with each party, Party A and Party B, holding one copy for compliance. (9) This contract shall be implemented within three months from the date of approval by the Ministry of Railways and the Construction Department of Zhejiang Province. (10) Matters not covered in the joint transportation between Party A and Party B may be supplemented or amended with the consent of both parties. (11) The validity period of this contract is one year from the date of implementation. If neither party proposes any amendments three months before the expiration date, it may continue to be implemented for another year, and this shall be done at the expiration of each term thereafter. (August 27)

▲ Tobacco and Alcohol License Tax The tobacco and alcohol license tax in Jiangsu Province is now ordered by the Provincial Government to be handled by the Ministry of Finance. The county tax bureau was won by Yan Yihe from Wujin through bidding and has arrived in the county to take over the matter. The bureau address is still located in Shengze Town, which belongs to the county.

Changzhou 78

▲ Pledge to Exterminate Traitors Group Warns Silk and Cloth Industry Since the establishment of the Blood Soul Anti-Traitor Group in Wu County, it has been extremely active in patriotic work. On the evening of the 26th, a youth suddenly came to the Silk and Cloth Industry Association with a letter and left after delivering it. The association opened it and found that it was a warning letter from the Pledge to Exterminate Traitors Group. The letter contained a bullet and a small package of shrapnel, and it pointed out that Sheng Taichang, Qian Tai Tan, Heng Shun Tai, and other families had gone to Shanghai to order a large batch of "enemy goods." The association immediately mimeographed the original letter and notified all colleagues on the 27th, including Sheng Taichang and other families, and declared in the Wu County newspaper on the 28th that they would not buy or sell "enemy goods."

▲ Various Public Groups Oppose the Transfer of the Disabled Soldiers' Hospital to Changzhou The various public groups in Wu County previously stated that because wounded soldiers gathered, misunderstandings often occurred with the people. They had repeatedly presented requests to military and political organs for relief. Now the wounded soldiers' hospital has been ordered to be revoked, and there is news that the Suzhou Disabled Soldiers' Hospital will be transferred to Changzhou. They deeply fear that there will be adverse consequences for local security. Yesterday, they sent a telegram to their fellow villagers in Beijing, and transferred it to the military and political authorities to sincerely explain and approve the cancellation. ▲ The Chief of the County Court is Replaced Lei Renlong, the chief of the Wu County Court, was accused of multiple offenses. The Ministry of Judicial Administration sent a commissioner to Changzhou to investigate secretly. Yesterday (27th), the Ministry dismissed Lei Renlong from his post and ordered him to be investigated. Cui Yun was appointed to take over the post.

Wuxi 79

▲ New Public Security Bureau Chief Arrives in Wuxi Hua Pu, the chief of the Wuxi County Public Security Bureau, was dismissed due to a case. Zhao, the Director of the Department of Civil Affairs, submitted it to the Provincial Government for discussion and resolution, and Wu Dexin was appointed to take over. After Wu was appointed, he came to Wuxi by night train the night before and met with County Chief Chen and Chief Hua. Hua has ordered the department to rush to handle the handover, which is scheduled to be implemented on September 1st. ▲ The Righteous Army of the 19th Route Goes North to Resist the Enemy After the Shanghai War broke out, patriots from all over the country rushed to join the 19th Route Army and were willing to be vanguards. Commander Cai allocated them to Weng Zhaoyuan, the brigade commander of the 156th Brigade of the 78th Division, and compiled them into the accompanying volunteer army, forming three major teams. When the 78th Division was transferred to Wuxi, it also taught the team field combat skills. The brigade held a graduation ceremony on June 10th and dispersed back to their original places. However, a part of them followed Brigade Commander Weng to Fujian to suppress bandits. There was also a part of them who volunteered to go to the Northeast to recover lost territory. They reorganized the accompanying volunteer army of the 156th Brigade and were still stationed in Huishan, actively training. Recently, seeing the urgent situation in Rehe, the team decided to go north to kill the enemy. The leader of the team, Li Xiangheng (from Jilin), sent a letter to General Zhu Zishu, discussing with Zhang Xueliang the issue of allowing passage and providing assistance with military salaries and equipment. They also signed and received a combined car passport and ticket from the Ministry of Military Affairs, and entrusted the Wuxi Station to prepare the vehicles. Yesterday, they all departed and went to Nanjing and then to the north.

Yangzhou 80

▲ Difficulty in Raising Funds for Relief of Transport Workers Previously, County Chief Yang received an order from the province to borrow cash using Busy Canal borrowing vouchers to relieve transport workers. He convened a meeting of representatives from the Central Bank, Bank of China, Bank of Communications, and money shops to borrow 18,000 yuan, half in silver and half in cash. Later, the three banks asked their head offices for instructions separately and did not receive approval. The money shops also encountered difficulties and successively replied to the county government, requesting exemption from apportionment. It is learned that County Chief Yang believed that the transport workers were in dire straits. Yesterday, he sent separate letters to the silver and money industries, asking them to consider the importance of the transport workers and reduce their burden by 6,000 yuan each. Furthermore, the voucher was guaranteed by the road construction mu tax and was guaranteed to be paid in full with interest by the end of December of this year, when the next busy season would have started collecting. It is not yet known whether the two industries will be able to borrow the money as requested.

Zhenjiang 81

▲ Establishment of Jiangsu Provincial Cooperative Association In order to connect feelings and jointly study cooperative theory, cooperative business instructors from all counties in Jiangsu Province specially organized the Jiangsu Provincial Cooperative Association. Yesterday afternoon at 3 o'clock, the inaugural meeting was held at the Zhenjiang County Party Department. More than one hundred party and government representatives and members attended. Liu Yongrun, a member, reported on the organization motivation and preparation process of the association on behalf of the members. Next, Lu Shiling, a representative of the Provincial Party Department, gave a speech, saying that previous mass movements were only temporary bursts of energy, but the public work movement was more sustainable. He also said that in the past, the farmer movement and the worker movement mostly went astray. Only the cooperative movement is a genuine movement to improve the economy of farmers and workers. Zhang Jizhou, a representative of the Department of Industry, gave a speech, saying that the most difficult problem to solve at present is the economic problem, and the most peaceful and appropriate way to solve the economic problem is the cooperative movement. Most of you here are practitioners of the cooperative movement. This time, the organization of the Jiangsu Cooperative Association is established. Its mission and responsibility not only relate to the future of Jiangsu cooperation, but also relate to the progress of all undertakings in Jiangsu Province. Therefore, I hope that after the organization of this association is established, it will not only be a formality, but will be put into practice. Li Qing, a representative of the County Party Department, gave a speech, saying that now various groups and organizations are united but not working, or working but not united. I hope that the comrades of your association will avoid this problem. Finally, members Qi Xifu, Ji Zhongru, and others gave speeches. After the meeting, they went to the Department of Industry to hold a discussion meeting.

▲ The Department of Finance Thoroughly Investigates Tax Evasion The busy canal tax in our country has accumulated too many malpractices over the years, and it is impossible to rectify it for a while, so that the people are full of complaints, and the government is also at a loss, watching the granaries, and greedily embezzling as much as possible. In the past two years, due to the exposure of the people and the severe punishment of the government, the wind of corruption has been slightly reduced. Previously, tax evasion cases were also discovered in Zhenjiang, which caused a sensation for a while. It is now heard that the county government has summoned the plaintiff and defendant for interrogation. With each side sticking to its own words, it is impossible to know the truth. It is not enough to check the deposits of previous years to clarify the truth. Therefore, the Department of Finance has been requested to select commissioners to supervise the checking of deposits to show caution and clarify the truth. Now the Department of Finance, in addition to instructing the county government to allow it, has also sent Xu Ruzhen to supervise and urge the Finance Bureau to check in detail year by year, and report truthfully.

▲ The Agency for Manufacturing Red Pills is Cracked Xi Enxiang, the acting inspector of the Fifth Division of the Third Branch of the Provincial Public Security Bureau, cracked a red pill manufacturing agency in a thatched house near Dengyun Temple at 3 am yesterday. Two people who manufactured red pills, Chu Yongxiang and Huang Changqin, were arrested. A machine, more than one hundred red pills, and many bags of medicinal powder were found in the house of Xu, a mother and son. They were escorted to the branch bureau and transferred to the general bureau for interrogation.

Nantong 82

▲ Director of Stamp Tax Bureau Replaced Hu Zuochu, the director of the Nantong Stamp Tax Bureau, was dismissed for a shortage of 8,000 yuan. Zhou Xinyuan was appointed to take over and took over on the 26th.

▲ Liang Guanying Thoroughly Investigates the Case of Extortion After Liang Guanying led his troops away from Suzhou to Anhui, he issued a notice to the counties, allowing those who had been harassed by his subordinates to report. Wu Hui, the former chief inspector stationed in Tong, was reported by the victims for abusing his power and extorting. Wu Zhonghui has been detained in Shucheng. Liang sent a commissioner to investigate the case to thoroughly investigate it.

▲ Problems with the Dismantling of the Nantong-Hai'an-Qidong Long-Distance Telephone Line The Jiangsu Bureau of Electrical Administration of the Ministry of Communications ordered the Nantong, Hai'men, and Jiulong Telegraph Bureaus to quickly dismantle the long-distance telephone line privately set up by the Hai Cong Company in the three counties of Nantong, Hai'an, and Qidong, because it hindered the state-owned business. The three county chiefs have now presented a report from the Tonghaiqi Industrial Special Police Team, stating that the long-distance telephone line is related to the joint defense of the three counties, and requested that it be exempted from demolition. The telegraph bureau has already submitted a report to the Bureau of Electrical Administration for instructions. ▲ The Director of the County Public Security Bureau is Dismissed Wu Yizeng, the director of the Nantong County Public Security Bureau, has been repeatedly reported to the province by the local people for various offenses, including abusing his power and extorting. The province has now dismissed Wu and appointed Chen Yizhong to succeed him.

Hangzhou 83

▲ Relief for Robbed Villagers in Shaoxing Wangwanxie Village, Shaoxing, was looted by bandits last month, and the villagers suffered losses. After Tang Rixin, the county magistrate of the county, reported to the province, Chairman Lu confirmed the facts and sent officials with funds to the village to distribute relief and find ways to help the villagers. In addition, Qingyuan, which borders Min Province in eastern Zhejiang, was harassed by bandits from Fujian, who kidnapped people for ransom. The provincial government yesterday consulted the Fujian government, instructing the Songping and Lian counties to expedite the investigation and clear the bandits, and ordered the commander of the bandit suppression in Zhejiang and Fujian to investigate and eliminate the banditry.

Xiaoshan 84

▲ Cotton Harvest is Poor, Early Rice is Bountiful Since the 23rd, Xiaoshan has experienced continuous wind and rain, and most of the mature cotton in Nansha has been blown down, resulting in a sharp decline in the harvest. In addition, the autumn silkworms are only hatching, and they have also been affected by the uneven weather. However, the early rice can be harvested, and the harvest is very good, with more than 2.5 dan per mu, which is unprecedented in recent years.

▲ Water Conservancy Bureau Surveys Qiantang River Dike The dikes along the Qiantang River in Xiaoshan have been in danger due to the continuous autumn rain and the rising autumn tide, which is very strong. The Water Conservancy Bureau sent personnel to survey and clearly ordered the workers to rush to repair them, so as to ensure that there will be no water disaster. It is said that the Tan Tou area in Kanxi must be actively repaired, otherwise the consequences will be unimaginable, because cracks have been found in the dikes due to the impact of the tides before and after the Mid-Autumn Festival.

Education News

Important News Zhu Jingnong Goes to Hunan to Take Office 85

▲ Leaving Beijing for Hankou and then Hunan Today

Since the government announced that Zhu Jingnong would be a member of the Hunan Provincial Government and concurrently the Director of the Department of Education, the Hunan authorities have repeatedly sent letters and telegrams urging Zhu to take office. Zhu arrived in Beijing on the 27th and had a face-to-face discussion with Minister Zhu Liuxian of the Ministry of Education on everything. It was decided that he would leave Beijing for Hankou today (29th), and then transfer to Hunan from Hankou. Zhu's plan for educational administration in Hunan will be determined after he arrives in Hunan and sees the local situation. However, in private conversations, he plans to develop child-centered education as much as possible in elementary schools in accordance with the Kuomintang's program. In middle schools, he will pay attention to livelihood education (in accordance with the measures submitted by the National Government to the National Conference on paying attention to livelihood education), such as career guidance, vocational training, etc. In universities, he plans to follow the methods prescribed by the Ministry of Education without making any changes. In addition, he will pay attention to physical education, and plans to imitate the German method of training young people's physical education, hiking and climbing mountains every week to exercise young people's physique. At the same time, he will pay attention to school aesthetics, especially for girls' schools, such as painting, sculpture, Xiang embroidery, etc. As for the entire educational administration plan, it will be decided after arriving in Hunan, considering the actual local conditions and adapting to local conditions. It is also heard that Zhu believes that administrative officials should not advance or retreat with political officials, so he will not make many changes to the staff of the Hunan Education Department.

The Second Day of the China Social Education Annual Conference 86

The first annual meeting of the China Social Education Society was held in Hangzhou the day before. The opening ceremony has been recorded in this newspaper. The following is a record of the meeting on the second day.

▲ Morning Meeting The meeting was still held in the Zhejiang Provincial Library at 8:00 am on the 25th. Sixty-two members, including Yu Qingtang, attended. Chairman Peng Baichuan reported that the first general meeting yesterday afternoon decided to assign all proposals to four groups for review. Now, the review of each case will be submitted to the general meeting for public discussion. A. Administrative Group. (1) Original proposal 8. The People's Education Universities in various provinces should be compared to normal schools, and high school classes should be attached to meet the urgent needs of talent creation. Review comments: Refer to the professional course methods of the Jiangsu Provincial Education Institute to meet urgent needs, and link the professional course curriculum with the university curriculum so that graduates of the professional course who aspire to further their studies can continue their research without attaching high school classes. Discussion results: (1) Review comments dismissed. (2) The original proposal was revised to suggest that provinces should respectively prepare to set up people's education teacher training classes at the high school level to meet urgent needs. (2) Original proposal 10. Please ask the education departments of various provinces to increase the number of people's education guidance commissioners in comparison with the status of provincial supervisors, so as to supervise and promote progress. Review comments: The title was changed to submit a request to the Ministry of Education to order various provinces and cities to increase the number of social education instructors in comparison with the status of supervisors, so as to supervise and benefit the social education case. The discussion results were passed according to the review comments. (3) Original proposal 11. A request to the Ministry of Education to order the social education authorities of the education organs of various provinces and counties to employ people with rich social education experience or specialized talents. Original proposal 12. A request to the Ministry of Education to order the education departments of various provinces to inform the people's education halls and other places to give priority to employing graduates of the people's schools. Review comments: The two cases were combined for discussion, and the title was changed to submit a request to the Ministry of Education to order the social education service personnel of the social education administrative organs of various provinces and cities to employ people with rich social education experience or specialized training.

Basketball Game: 20th Army Wins Over Fire Beacon 88

▲ Fire Beacon's basketball skills are mediocre.

▲ The visiting team's strength is not weak.

——Result: 40 to 11——

▲ Today's tennis match against Lingnan.

The basketball team of the 20th Army of Sichuan played against the Fire Beacon team at the China Basketball Hall last night at 7 o'clock. It was found that the Fire Beacon team is an average team in the fifth division of Group B of the Shanghai Basketball Association. The Sichuan Army's strength is quite considerable, comparable to the teams in the second division of Group B of the Shanghai Basketball Association. Therefore, the situation in last night's battle was quite disparate. As a result, the Sichuan Army won by a large margin of 40 to 11.

▲ After the start of the first half, the Sichuan Army was extremely active. Their passing and shooting were just right, so the score increased steadily. When they scored 13 points, the Fire Beacon team finally opened the scoring. The result of the first half was 17 points for the Sichuan Army and only 2 points for the Fire Beacon team.

▲ In the second half, the Sichuan Army's momentum became even stronger, and they were successful in their attacks, unstoppable. Although the Fire Beacon team tried hard to counterattack, they were ultimately ineffective due to their weakness. Therefore, the score difference remained quite large. In the second half, the score became 23 to 9. The Sichuan Army has quite average talent, although their coordination is slightly lacking, each person is quite hardworking, and their shooting is also confident. In yesterday's game, left forward Pei Songze scored a total of 17 points. The results are as follows:

A Wonderful Scene from the Summer Football Tournament: Huadong Won Against Qingnian Yesterday 91

▲ Both teams have good skills and a lot of exciting competition.

▲ Qingnian scored first, but ultimately lost 1-4.

With the golden breeze and the bright sun shining on the green grass of the China Baseball Field, Huadong and Qingnian played a summer football match yesterday at 5 pm. The beautiful time and scenery created a pleasant atmosphere. Both teams had similar skills and outstanding talents. They were the best teams in the summer football tournament and had the qualifications to win the championship. Meeting on the road, there was naturally a fierce battle. Qingnian's powerful momentum was awe-inspiring, and they scored first. As a result, they lost 1-4 to Huadong. The spectators were all satisfied and exclaimed that it was a spectacular sight. The excellent performance of both teams was unprecedented in the summer tournament. In addition, the results of the other two groups were (1) Starlight won against Qiangnan, 4-1, and (2) Qinghua won against Dajiang, 7-1. Qinghua has not yet been defeated, and there is still hope for the future. The lineups and match situation of Huadong vs. Qingnian are described below.

▲ Huadong Team

Qian Jingyong

Wang Changying Wu Youlin Tu Kaiyuan

Lu Zhongen Li Ning Hu Youcheng (Yang Renwei up, Dong Xiaopei down)

Chen Xianglong Mao Honggui (Shi Jinsheng up, Xi Qiaosheng down)

▲ Qingnian Team

Zheng Liankun (Xin Ziliang down, Cao Chuyun up)

Zhang Yangmu Xu Buyun

Li Wenqing Zheng Liankun (Zhu Wenkui up, Wang Fengchun down)

Zhang Pengnian (Zhu Wenlan down, Ma Wenjun up, Shen Jinda down, Gu Yifei Zhu Xiaoyun)

▲ Qingnian takes the lead. The referee, He Kehui, blows the whistle to start the match. Huadong kicks off and attacks first. The momentum is smooth, approaching the enemy's goal, but they are unsuccessful. Qingnian suddenly rushes towards Huadong's goal like a storm. Huadong is caught off guard, and the defense is negligent and improper. Qingnian's Xiao Rong and Gu Yifei advance at the same time. Huadong's Chen Xianglong fails to defend in time, and Gu Yifei rushes to the goal and succeeds in one fell swoop. The audience's spirits are lifted, and Huadong is shocked. This happened within the first ten minutes.

▲ Huadong immediately returns the favor. In terms of momentum, Huadong often has the upper hand. Observers believe that although Qingnian is brave, they may not be able to protect their goal from being breached. Indeed, within five minutes, Huadong returned a goal to Qingnian. When Huadong surrounded Qingnian's goal on all sides, Qian Jingyong sent out a corner kick. Tu Kaiyuan received it effectively, and Hu Youcheng managed to shoot the ball into the goal. Even with superb goalkeeping skills, there was no remedy.

▲ Qian Jingyong's power. Half an hour later, Huadong's Hu Youcheng scored another goal. The credit for this goal should be given to Hu's kick, but Qian Jingyong's power cannot be forgotten. Tu Kaiyuan, positioned in the center, sent the ball far to the left corner of the boundary. Left winger Qian Jingyong was also originally in the center, but he managed to break through the enemy's defense and pass the ball in. His running was as fast as a dragon colt, and the audience's shouts and cheers added to his momentum. His aura was invincible. In the first half, Huadong took the lead with a score of 2-1.

▲ Qiaosheng also scores a goal. In the second half, Huadong's momentum became even better. The activity of the forwards, the bravery of the midfielders, and the firmness of the defenders all made Qingnian pale in comparison. Huadong's Dong Xiaopei once attacked the goal, and it seemed that the ball had entered the goal, but it was blocked and saved by the Qingnian goalkeeper. One person was disappointed, and the other was surprised. However, Huadong's military power was strong, and although Qingnian tried hard to resist, it was difficult to take care of all sides. Over time, Xi Qiaosheng received Qian Jingyong's pass and attacked into the goal, making the score 3-1.

▲ Jingyong's header skills. For a long time, the two armies competed, and the situation was stable. Qingnian's forwards could hardly cross the line. The momentum of the ball was concentrated on one side. Fortunately, Qingnian's defenders were still working hard and could turn danger into safety. Three minutes before the end of the match, the two armies fought fiercely in front of the Qingnian goal. Tu Kaiyuan once shot fiercely, and the ball bounced back from the crossbar with great force. The sound was like a cannon. Although it did not enter the goal, it made Qingnian suffer a false alarm. However, from false to real, Qian Jingyong suddenly headed the ball into the goal. There was little time left, and the match ended. Huadong won 4-1.

▲ The veteran's power is undiminished. The Huadong team has many famous generals from Shanghai and is not weak. Yesterday, they showed more distinctive characteristics. People like Qian Jingyong, Tu Kaiyuan, Dong Xiaopei, Xi Qiaosheng, and Hu Youcheng all had good performances. Li Ning made his debut yesterday, taking care of all sides and showing the momentum of one man guarding the pass, and ten thousand men not being able to pass. His achievements on the battlefield are invaluable. Defenders Wang Changying and Chen Xianglong defended effectively and made few mistakes. Goalkeeper Lu Zhongen was as stable as Mount Tai, and did not need to use his hands and feet. The team was united in spirit, and their coordination was also good. They seem to have great hope for the summer championship. As for the Qingnian team, they have many new and promising generals. The team is average, and their offense and defense are excellent. There is great hope for the future.

Financial: Last Week, the Gold Market Suddenly Turned Downward, Plunging by 24 Taels, Breaking Through the 700 Tael Mark 93

Last week, the gold market experienced a sharp decline, breaking through the 700 tael mark. However, there were no excessive fluctuations on a daily basis, with only occasional fluctuations of less than 10 taels. Since the silver market reported a decline at the beginning of the week, and the exchange rate was secretly flat, the price failed to rise due to the increasing tension caused by the Japanese invasion. The opening price for October was the same as the previous Saturday, at 717 taels, followed by 719 taels and 3 qian (the highest price of the week). Afterwards, the overseas silver market fluctuated, and the exchange rate between the UK and the US rebounded slightly after a few days of small gains. As a result, the gold market entered a state of hovering, fluctuating around 710 taels. As the international economic conference gradually made progress, the United States had already sent representatives, and the silver prices in the UK and the US tended to rise. The Shanghai market was also firm, but the supply from Chinese merchants exceeded demand, and hedging transactions were minimal, as they were not cost-effective. Therefore, both sides were short, and the selling pressure from major players was strong, and the market suddenly showed a decline, with dark clouds looming, plunging by more than 20 taels. On Saturday, a new low of 691 taels and 8 qian was suddenly seen. The entire week saw a retracement of 27 taels and 5 qian. Compared with the previous Saturday, the total decline was 24 taels (having fallen for five consecutive weeks, a total of about 54 taels). The difference between the opening and closing prices was also 24 taels. As for large bars and silver prices, they rebounded slightly, as the UK/US exchange rate frequently rose (by half a unit). The domestic market followed suit, and gold merchants initially delivered slightly, but continued to sell relentlessly. The UK gold price rose by 5.625, and the US gold price continued to rise by 8.125. However, the exchange rate was reversed, with the UK against the US continuing to fall by 75, and the US against the UK falling slightly by 375. The gold closing price was initially pressed down by 70 taels, and then by more than 80 taels. However, the hedging of forward US dollars was about 50 taels apart, and the spot market was still flat. The Central Bank absorbed and sold US dollars. According to a survey, there were more gold exchange contracts than before, estimated at 25,000 contracts. The long positions were mainly held by Yuanxingyong, Qianchangxiang, Yifengyong, etc., while the short positions were held by Hengxing, Tongtaichang, Hengxingyuan, Yuanmaoyong, etc. According to Reuters on the 28th (yesterday), the price of large silver bars rose slightly again. Observing the situation, the gold market may still undergo a change. The high and low prices of the UK and US silver markets and exchange rates are listed below:

The Securities Market Remains Pessimistic, Bond Prices Experienced a Slight Decline Last Week, with Sluggish Trading and Low Volume 95

Over the past week (from August 22nd to 27th), the bond market situation at the local Chinese Securities Exchange remained quite lackluster. Spot market trading continued to be extremely sparse, with a total weekly turnover of only 45,000 yuan. Among these, bond transactions accounted for only 4,000 to 5,000 yuan. Although the futures market did not experience significant changes, it was approaching the end of the month, nearing settlement. Therefore, there were more swap and liquidation transactions from various parties, making the market atmosphere not entirely desolate. Daily trading slightly increased compared to the previous period, with a peak of approximately 6.7 million yuan on the first day of the week. On other days, trading mainly ranged around 4.7 to 4.8 million yuan. Only on the weekend, trading in the August series was temporarily suspended in preparation for settlement, resulting in a very quiet market with only 1.4 million yuan traded in the September series. The total weekly trading volume for various bonds was 26.905 million yuan, exceeding the previous week by more than 7 million yuan. Among these, the Disbandment Bonds, Salt Tax Bonds, and Unified Tax Bonds remained relatively active. The Salt Tax Bonds saw 2.585 million yuan traded in the August series and 3.4005 million yuan in the September series. The Disbandment Bonds saw 2.205 million yuan traded in the August series and 3.33 million yuan in the September series. The Unified Tax Bonds saw 2.015 million yuan traded in the August series and 2.16 million yuan in the September series. Other bonds, such as the 1920 Customs Bonds, saw 1.63 million yuan traded in the August series and 1.45 million yuan in the September series. The 1919 Customs Bonds saw 1.195 million yuan traded in the August series and 885,000 yuan in the September series. The 1919 Benevolent Bonds saw 845,000 yuan traded in the August series and 775,000 yuan in the September series. The Reorganization Bonds saw 975,000 yuan traded in the August series and 360,000 yuan in the September series. The Customs Bonds saw 260,000 yuan traded in the August series and 75,000 yuan in the September series. The 1926 Consolidated Bonds only saw trading in the August series, with the 1926 Consolidated Bonds at 120,000 yuan and the 1926 Bonds at 25,000 yuan. The financial market was inactive. Regarding the price fluctuations of various bonds during the past week, although the international situation was generally favorable and the domestic situation was considered stable, the overall environment could be said to be slightly better than before. However, the situation in the Northeast remained concerning. Although the invasion of Jehol had temporarily ceased, the exposed ambitions indicated that the future prospects between China and Japan remained bleak. Therefore, although bond market trading was slightly more active due to swap and liquidation activities, investor sentiment remained unchanged. Under the current circumstances, both buyers and sellers were taking a wait-and-see approach. Furthermore, the low prices in the spot market made sellers extremely reluctant. Market transactions were sporadic, and large investors rarely engaged in large-scale transactions. As a result, the supply and demand situation did not change significantly, and price trends fluctuated within a narrow range. There was no consistent upward or downward trend, and the stagnant situation remained unchanged. Reviewing the price movements, Monday saw a relatively significant drop of about one yuan. On Tuesday, Wednesday, and Thursday, prices generally hovered and gradually strengthened. Friday saw a slight decline, and Saturday saw a drop of about seven to eight jiao. Overall, the decline outweighed the increase compared to the previous week. The September series of the Disbandment Bonds and the 1920 Customs Bonds each rose by approximately 1.4 yuan, while the September series of the 1919 Customs Bonds, Benevolent Bonds, 1920 Bonds, Consolidated Bonds, Salt Tax Bonds, etc., each fell by about one yuan. Other bonds experienced price changes of about half a yuan or less. Judging from the market situation, the current state remains extremely chaotic, and the future prospects are not yet overly optimistic. Silk and Tea: The Silk Market Flourished Last Week 98

▲ Scarce Inventory Cannot Meet Demand:: European Demand Remains Strong, Shortages Cause Prices to Rise

▲ The Best Situation in Nearly Two Years:: Future Prospects Gradually Appear Optimistic

Last week, the Shanghai foreign firm silk market almost flourished. European and American silk weavers, seeing that the world economy was gradually recovering and silk product sales were improving, and that cocoon production in various silk-producing countries was poor this year, with production not meeting sales, and fearing a silk shortage in the future, began to buy spot and futures silk. Suddenly, the market atmosphere became bullish and silk prices rose sharply. During the past week, overseas yellow and white silk transactions remained strong. The rising trend in the New York and Lyon raw silk markets had not stopped, and Yokohama silk also continued to rise. Chinese silk merchants believed that raw materials were scarce and predicted that raw silk production would not meet demand. They maintained a firm attitude, believing that shortages and price increases were a natural trend in the market. Spot and futures silk transactions remained brisk during the past week, and prices generally trended upwards. Spot silk exports reached over 2,000 bales, which was the best situation in nearly two years. Future prospects gradually appeared optimistic.
