Paper Money Tax Resolved 122

▲ Tax Amount: 3.06 Million Yuan

▲ All Banks Have Fully Paid

The National News Agency reports that there has been much speculation and confusion about the collection of the paper money tax. Yesterday, a reporter from the National News Agency visited the responsible personnel of the Ministry of Finance to inquire about the truth of the matter. They were kind enough to make the following statement:

The National Government promulgated the Paper Money Regulations on August 1, 20. The regulations stipulate that the banks issuing paper money should have 60% in cash and 40% in marketable securities as reserve funds. A portion of the securities should be taxed at 2.5%, and a portion of the cash is naturally tax-free. The total paper money tax rate is only 1% of the total amount issued. The banks in Shanghai that issue paper money firmly acknowledge that the government has the reason to collect the paper money tax. At the same time, they believe that the Japanese army's invasion of Shanghai and the floods throughout the country have led to financial stagnation and commercial depression. They generally believe that the tax rate set by the government is too high and request that the original 2.5% be reduced to 1.25%. The Ministry of Finance's opinion is that commercial conditions should be considered, and the country's finances should also be taken into account. The tax rate can be reduced in the future, but for this year, the laws and regulations that the country has promulgated must be implemented. As a result of the consultations, the banks have a long sense of patriotism and take the overall situation into account. They have paid the full tax amount of 3.06 million yuan.

Song and Cai Fly to Beijing This Morning 123

▲ Departure Delayed Yesterday Due to Engine Damage

The Central News Agency reports that Mr. Song Ziwen, acting President of the Executive Yuan, received a telegram from Chairman Chiang from Wuhan the day before yesterday, urging him to immediately accompany Minister of Transportation Chen Mingshu and General Commander of the 19th Route Army Cai Tingkai to Beijing to discuss national affairs. Mr. Song originally planned to accompany Mr. Cai to Beijing on Mr. Song's own Sikorsky aircraft yesterday morning. However, it was found that the tail rotation of the aircraft was not working properly during the test flight yesterday morning. For the sake of prudence, the pilot immediately drove the aircraft to the Longhua Airport for repairs. As of 2:00 p.m., the repairs had not been completed, so Mr. Song was unable to go to Beijing yesterday. The departure has been rescheduled for 6:00 a.m. this morning, when he will fly to Beijing with General Commander Cai. Minister of Transportation Chen Mingshu was unable to accompany him due to other commitments.

Sino-Foreign Commercial Treaties Remain Valid for Three Years 124

▲ Sino-French Commercial Treaty Has Expired But Has Not Been Implemented

▲ Japanese Treaty Has Exceeded Thirty Years and is Not Allowed to be Revised

The new commercial treaties that our country revised with Belgium, Italy, Denmark, Portugal, Spain, Turkey, France, Poland, and other countries in 17 and 18 years will expire this year after three years. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs has not yet notified the countries to revise them again. Foreigners say that they will continue to be valid for three years. However, the Sino-French Vietnam Commercial Treaty has been in effect for three years since its approval, but the French have not yet implemented it. The Sino-Japanese Commercial Treaty has exceeded 30 years, and the Japanese have not allowed it to be revised. In addition, for those that have not expired, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs will continue to revise them when they expire. The following is a record of the news obtained by the reporter of the New Sound News Agency:

▲ Continued Validity for Three Years The new commercial treaties that the Ministry of Foreign Affairs revised with Belgium, Italy, Denmark, Portugal, and Spain between November and December of the 17th year and the commercial treaties that were concluded or revised with Turkey, France, and Poland between January, May, and September of the 18th year, except for the Sino-Polish Treaty, were mutually notified and approved by the governments of both countries in the 18th year and took effect. Currently, except for the Sino-French Commercial Treaty, which expires on the 16th of next month, and the Sino-Polish Commercial Treaty, which expires in the spring of next year, the others have expired one after another this year after three years. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs has not yet notified the above countries to propose revisions. A reporter from the New Sound News Agency inquired from the consulate that since neither party to the expired treaties has proposed revisions, the treaty will remain valid for another three years. According to international practice, treaties are mostly established with a validity period of three years. After the expiration, if neither party proposes revisions, they will continue to be valid for another three years and do not need to be notified.

▲ Japan Refuses to Revise The Sino-Japanese Commercial Treaty was signed in the 22nd year of Guangxu and has been in effect for nearly 40 years. China has expired three times (according to the old rate set by China and foreign countries, the term is 10 years), but the Japanese side still refuses to propose revisions. The Japanese side is taking the excuse that the six-month consultation period has expired (according to the treaty, revisions should be discussed within six months, and if they are not completed, they will continue to be valid for 10 years) and requesting an extension of 10 years. Currently, the treaty has exceeded 34 years and has not been revised. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs has long announced that all countries whose treaties have expired and have not been able to revise new treaties are considered to be countries without treaties and will be treated with the temporary measures announced in the 17th year.

▲ France Does Not Implement The Sino-French Vietnam Land Commercial Treaty and the Sino-French Beijing Supplementary Commercial Treaty. In July of the 17th year, a note was sent to the French ambassador to open negotiations. After a year, the Sino-French Beijing Supplementary Commercial Treaty was abolished on May 16, 1929, and revised and signed as the Sino-French Vietnam Land Commercial Treaty. After being approved by the governments of both countries, it took effect on September 16 of the same year. It will expire on the 16th of next month, after three years. However, the French side is delaying implementation on the pretext that the Gui Army destroyed the French Consulate in Hankou last year and the refund of import taxes in Yunnan. After the Ministry of Foreign Affairs explained to France, the French side fully understood, but the regulations on the mutual benefit goods list between the two countries have prevented it from being realized. It is heard that the authorities are in the process of carrying it out.

The Anti-War Alliance Held Two Meetings Yesterday and Declared Its Closure Last Night 125

▲ Appointed Ma Xiangbo and 14 Others as Honorary Committee Members

▲ Appointed Wu Daquan and 56 Others as Standing Committee Members

The Standing Committee Will Be Established Today

The Anti-Civil War Grand Alliance held its second and third meetings yesterday morning. It was decided to establish branches in various provinces, cities, counties, and overseas Chinese locations to recruit members and carry out the anti-civil war movement. At the afternoon meeting, 57 standing committee members, including Wu Daquan, and 15 honorary committee members, including Ma Xiangbo, were elected. The conference closed last night and issued a declaration. The first meeting of the standing committee will be held at the Bankers' Association at 3:00 p.m. today. The following is a record of the news:

Second Meeting in the Morning 126

▲ Mr. Lin's Speech The meeting was declared open at 9:00 a.m. The chairman, Wang Xiaolai, respectfully read Dr. Sun Yat-sen's will and performed the ceremony. Then, the chairman, Lin Kanghou, reported on the meeting of the Review Committee and the Preparatory Committee. He said that the presidium of the conference and the preparatory committee had tried their best to make everything simple and clear, so that the cessation of civil war could be effectively implemented. Some people doubt whether the alliance has any political background and whether Shanghai has been contracted to do it. In fact, the alliance is purely an organization of all sectors of society who yearn for the cessation of civil war and has no background. The original initiators were the four organizations in Shanghai, and the meeting place was in Shanghai, so it was more convenient and enthusiastic for Shanghai people to participate. However, this only shows their enthusiasm for the cessation of war. As for the implementation plan, as soon as the general association and branch organizations are established, they will be able to exert their influence and eliminate civil war. Yesterday, we received telegrams from the Honolulu Chinese Chamber of Commerce and the Chinese United Association, congratulating the opening of the alliance and joining the alliance. Then, he explained that the Yantai Beer Company donated beer and the Yick Loong Watson Company donated soda water, which were both national product merchants expressing their enthusiastic support for the cessation of civil war. Then, he reported on today's agenda and the inspection of the city's chamber of commerce boy scouts by the representatives at noon, and asked the Datong Music Society to play national music.

▲ Review Report Chen Liting, chairman of the Proposal Review Committee, reported on the review of the proposals and received 85 formal proposals. There were many other opinions expressed in letters and declarations. Since they were not formal proposals, they were not included. All the proposals were divided into two categories in addition to the proposals of the Preparatory Committee, which were classified as the first category. The second category was the plan within the scope of the alliance's articles of association, including 61 proposals from Liang Shiyi and others. The third category was the plan outside the scope of the alliance's articles of association, including 24 proposals. Among them, many have both characteristics and have been listed separately.

The Review Committee believes that all the plans in categories 2 and 3 are of great value and asks you to discuss them in detail.

▲ Discussion Situation After the review report, according to the agenda, the discussion of the first category of proposals began. Ye Guansheng temporarily moved that the articles of association of the alliance should be revised and passed by the representative assembly. For a time, those who seconded and those who thought it was not necessary to revise and pass all stated their reasons. After an hour of discussion, the chairman, Wu Daquan, put it to a vote. As a result, the majority agreed to submit it to the assembly for passage. Lin Kanghou then read it item by item. Except for the assumption that the number of standing committee members in Article 7 was from 50 to 100, and the addition of Article 11, the rest were passed according to the original proposal. It was already 10:45 a.m. Then, the first category and the second category of proposals were discussed and passed, and they were handed over to the standing committee for separate implementation.

▲ Resolutions on Various Cases A. Review Report, First Category (1) Branches should be quickly borrowed from chambers of commerce or other legal organizations in various provinces, cities, counties, and overseas Chinese locations. The articles of association will be quickly formulated and handled by the Standing Committee. (2) The General Association and branches should quickly publish in newspapers and send people to recruit members. All organizations and individuals who have joined the initiators should also be introduced to members separately. (3) According to Article 2, Paragraph 1 of the Articles of Association, the General Association should quickly publish a "Cessation of Civil War" periodical on a regular basis and send it to the branch associations in various provinces and cities for distribution in the locations of the general and branch associations. Celebrities should be invited to give public speeches on "Cessation of Civil War" at any time. (4) According to Article 2, Paragraph 2 of the Articles of Association, the personnel of the General Association and branches should investigate at any time whether there are political disputes in various places that may cause civil war, and report them to the Standing Committee for prevention. (5) According to the provisions of Article 2, Paragraph 2 of the Articles of Association, the Standing Committee should adopt the proposals of the members and study the methods of peaceful cessation when civil war occurs, and may appoint members who are familiar with the situation in various places and industries as commissioners to study separately for temporary adoption by the Standing Committee. (6) The expenses of the General Association, according to Article 8 of the Articles of Association, are planned to be raised from the organizations and individuals who join. Each organization is free to determine the annual donation of 50 yuan to 500 yuan, and each individual is free to determine the annual donation of 5 yuan to 100 yuan. If the above donations are not enough for the use of the alliance, donations may be raised from organizations or individuals outside the alliance to supplement them. After this case was discussed and passed by the assembly, it was handed over to the Standing Committee for separate handling. B. Review Report, Second Category. 61 proposals from Liang Shiyi and others were passed by the assembly and handed over to the Standing Committee for handling.

▲ Formation of Nomination Committee The discussion continued until 11:20 a.m. The chairman, Wu Dingchang, announced that he was afraid that there would not be enough time to continue discussing the proposals and proposed to discuss the formation of the nomination committee in advance. It was decided to elect the seven members of the presidium as ex officio members, and then the presidium would appoint 14 people to form the nomination committee. When 14 people were appointed, Yu Rongqiao, Han Yangshan, Chen Peide, Li Gongpu, Shi Leiying, Liu Jichen, Zhu Xuefan, Huang Linsheng, Chen Liting, Liu Guangpei, Xu Jiqing, Chen Zheqing, Song An, and Ye Guansheng opened the nomination committee at 1:20 p.m.

Abolishing the Warring Factions Alliance Charter 127

Charter for the Abolition of the Civil War Grand Alliance: (Article 1) This conference is convened to launch a nationwide people's movement to abolish civil war because foreign aggression is rampant, stemming from internal strife, and internal excuses are rife, due to civil war. (Article 2) This Alliance's movement to abolish civil war shall proceed in the following order: (1) In peacetime, the Alliance

Page 15

should publish open letters or speeches, stating the evils of civil war and elucidating the benefits of peace. (2) If political disputes arise that are sufficient to cause civil war, the Alliance should advise both sides to trust any popular representative bodies (before formal national representative bodies are established, legally recognized civilian business groups can substitute) to mediate. Neither party shall absolutely resort to force to resolve the issue. (3) If, unfortunately, civil war does break out, all group members and individual members of the Alliance should unanimously refuse to cooperate and may even adopt peaceful and appropriate methods to stop it. (Article 3) This Alliance shall not engage in any other activities except for the movement to abolish civil war. (Article 4) Anyone who supports the aims of this Alliance, regardless of individual, group, gender, profession, or political party, may sign up as a member without needing an introduction and have their name publicly announced by the Alliance. (Article 5) The Alliance may establish a general affairs office in Shanghai and may establish branch offices at

necessary locations. (Article 6) The Alliance may establish several standing committee members, with a term of one year, to form a standing committee to deliberate and manage all affairs of the Alliance. Because of the large number of members and the vast area, it is difficult to convene a general meeting. For the sake of simple and convenient procedures, the number and selection of the first standing committee members shall be decided and publicly nominated by the initiators. From the second term onwards, the standing committee shall decide and publicly nominate them. If necessary, administrative staff may be appointed, also decided and selected by the standing committee. (Article 7) The Alliance may appoint several honorary members, nominated by the standing committee. (Article 8) The Alliance does not collect membership fees, and its funds may be raised through donations from supporting organizations and individuals, but it shall not request assistance from the central or local governments or any public institutions. (Article 9) All rules and regulations necessary for the Alliance's affairs shall be formulated by the standing committee. (Article 10) The Alliance's term of establishment is temporarily set at five years, but if no civil war occurs before the expiration of that period, and it is deemed unnecessary to continue the abolition movement, it may be dissolved early. (Article 11) This charter shall be implemented upon approval by the representative assembly and shall be amended in the same way.

▲ Meeting Situation: The Nominating Committee met at 1:30 PM, with the attendance of Chen Zheqing, Xu Jiluo, Chen Liting, Wang Xiaolai, Shi Yunying, Yang Meizhen, Liu Zongchen, Pu Yangshan, Lu Zhangyuan, Liu Zhanen, Chen Peide, Song An, Yu Rongqiao, Chen Shucheng, Ye Guansheng, Liu Guangpei, Lin Kanghou, Wu Daquan, Li Gongpu, and Huang Linsheng. Chen Liting served as chairman, and Yan E'sheng served as recorder. Three principles were resolved. Based on these principles, a total of fifty-seven standing committee members were proposed. The meeting adjourned at 2:30 PM.

▲ Principles Adopted: (1) Coverage of all provinces; (2) Inclusion of all professional groups; (3) Individuals with considerable reputation and influence in their local areas.

Afternoon Third Meeting 129

After performing the ceremonial rites, he reported on the Nominating Committee meeting and the nomination standards. He then announced the list of fifteen honorary members and fifty-seven standing committee members (recorded separately) and explained that as the Alliance's affairs expand, the number of honorary members and standing committee members will be increased at any time, in order to generate widespread power. He requested the assembly's approval, which was passed unanimously without objection.

▲ Discussion Situation: Continuing the discussion of proposals, the review committee, Chen Liting, first reported that there were twenty-five proposals, which were merged into the third category. The reason being that although the content was extremely valuable, some proposals were beyond the Alliance's capabilities, such as reorganizing the army. During the discussion, some people questioned the standard of the scope of civil war. After the review committee explained, "Non-bandit suppression military actions are considered civil war and are factually determined by the standing committee." Afterwards, someone raised the question of whether the suppression of communists constitutes civil war and how the Alliance should express its opinion on it. Chairman Lin Kanghou replied that it would be referred to the standing committee to solicit public opinion and make a decision. Subsequently, it was resolved that all third-category proposals would be referred to the standing committee for consideration and implementation. Later, Huang Jinghan and fifty-three others proposed a temporary motion on how to prevent the financial sector from recognizing and raising public bonds related to civil war. The proposers requested the assembly to send a telegram to all sectors, uniformly refusing to do so. Chairman Lin Kanghou and Wang Xiaolai explained separately that there was no need to send a telegram because any military personnel raising public bonds would always use construction as a pretext and would never openly admit to using it for civil war. Qian Xinzhi said that the initiating groups are the banking and money industry groups. As he works for a bank and has now joined the Alliance, he will never lend a single penny to civil war in the future (applause from the crowd). He also hoped to absorb all staff, students, and workers of the banking and money industry into the Alliance so that its power would be strong. Chairman Lin Kanghou decided that the standing committee should widely solicit the membership of the financial industry in various places to cut off the economic sources of civil war. There were also seven temporary motions, such as actively assisting the Northeast Volunteer Army, proposed by Chen Peide, Gong Yi, and others, all of which were referred to the standing committee.

Ministry of Railways Hosts Explanation Meeting for All Sectors on Responsible Transportation 134

▲ Yu Yan's Important Remarks

In order to clarify the doubts about the responsible transportation implemented by the Ministry of Railways starting on September 1st, the Ministry of Railways specially dispatched Yu Yan, Director of the Business Department, and Tan Yaozong, Assistant Director, to Shanghai. Yesterday afternoon at 3 PM, they hosted a public report at the Bank Association for all sectors. The details are recorded below:

▲ Attendees: Yu Yan, Director of the Business Department of the Ministry of Railways; Tan Yaozong, Assistant Director; Chen Xinghan, Director of the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Bureaus; Zheng Baozhao, Director of the Traffic Department. The guests included representatives from the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, the Bank of China, the Bank of Communications, the fresh meat industry, the silk reeling industry, the yarn industry, and other industry associations, as well as reporters from various newspapers and news agencies, totaling approximately several dozen people. They took their seats at 3:30 PM, with Director Yu serving as chairman. He respectfully read the Prime Minister's will, and then Assistant Director Tan Yaozong reported on the significance of implementing cargo transportation responsibility.

▲ Chairman's Opening Remarks: After the meeting began at 3 PM and ceremonial rites were performed, Chairman Yu Yan gave a speech, stating that the Ministry of Communications and military authorities had long established transportation regulations for railway transportation since the tenth year of the Republic, but due to the lack of responsibility for transportation, domestic goods could not circulate smoothly. Goods piled up like mountains in the production areas, and there were no goods for sale in the consumption areas. The lack of circulation of goods led to the decline of the commercial market, and the decline of the commercial market led to the stagnation of the social economy. The Ministry of Railways itself does not want to hide the fact that it is not developing. At the same time, the high transportation costs demanded by the transshipment companies also contributed to this. For example, on the Beijing-Ningbo Railway, the transportation cost for one car of 20 tons of goods from Tianjin to Ping is 140 yuan, but the same route costs 200 yuan when transshipped. Because the railway is not responsible, cargo owners have no choice but to hire boats and small carts themselves to transport their goods, which inevitably costs them more money. Now, since Minister Gu has taken office at the Ministry of Railways, in order to relieve the suffering of merchants and people, he has actively promoted responsible transportation, so that goods can flow smoothly, and the railway's own business can also rely on it for development. What could be more pleasing than achieving both at the same time? Therefore, today, I am grateful that representatives from all sectors have taken the time to attend. I would like to seize this opportunity to gather together and ask you to give your guidance to the Ministry's handling of responsible transportation.

▲ Assistant Director Tan's Report: After the chairman's speech, Tan Yaozong, Assistant Director of the Business Department of the Ministry of Railways, reported on the benefits of responsible transportation to cargo owners, the people, and the railway itself, stating, "Distinguished guests, Director Yu has just explained the meaning of responsible transportation, the relief it can bring to the suffering of merchants, and the importance of developing industry and commerce in great detail. Now, let me prove it with facts. What Director Yu said is real, not theoretical. It is indeed unreasonable for the railway to be irresponsible. If goods are handed over to boatmen or porters for transport to their destination and are lost midway, can they say they are not responsible? Therefore, the railway's lack of responsibility has resulted in undesirable consequences: (1) The transportation of goods with low profits and low prices is not dared by merchants due to the lack of responsibility, and neither the production area nor the consumption area benefits. The railway also has less transportation income. (2) Because the railway is not responsible, merchants choose to transport non-time-sensitive goods by other means. For example, in the thirteenth year of the Republic, grain was transported from the Northeast to Tianjin. Because the railway was not responsible, most merchants went from the Northeast to Dalian and then to Tianjin. By the seventeenth year of the Republic, the Beijing-Ningbo Railway, in order to remedy cargo transportation, specially worked with the Sidao and Shenhai railways to handle joint transportation, but the result was that the goods still went to the South Manchuria Railway. (3) The railway's transportation cannot be guaranteed, so transshipment companies take advantage of the situation to engage in profiteering, with countless malpractices, such as secretly selling cargo cars and extorting tips from porters, all adding an extra burden to cargo owners. Moreover, business is sluggish due to extortion. Now, let me tell you a precedent that will surely amaze you. The South Manchuria Railway's income per kilometer is 110,000 yuan per year, while our country's railways only earn 20,000 yuan, a difference of more than five times. The reason for this is entirely the relationship between responsibility and irresponsibility. Therefore, the Ministry of Railways is now actively promoting responsibility. On the one hand, it wants to develop the railway itself, and on the other hand, it wants to relieve the suffering of commercial transportation."

▲ Guests' Speeches: After Tan Yaozong finished his report, speeches were given by the guests, starting with Li Ruzhang, representative of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, and then Huo Baoshu of the Bank of Communications. The general idea was that responsible transportation is certainly well-intentioned, but the authorities should take strict precautions against the malpractice of station staff demanding bribes in small matters. Next, speeches were given by Jin Shaoqin of the Bank of China and Zhao Shuyong, representative of the press, which had much in common, saying that responsible transportation by the Ministry of Railways is certainly convenient for both the railway and cargo owners, but the transshipment industry must also be taken into consideration, otherwise the livelihood of the transshipment industry will inevitably be difficult. Finally, the chairman replied, saying that the Ministry of Railways has already instructed the staff of each road station to take precautions against the malpractice of transshipment and road bureau personnel in transportation, and although the transshipment industry will be affected, the smooth flow of cargo can lead to less profit and more transportation, and the transshipment industry will not decline because of the railway's responsible transportation. After the speech, the meeting adjourned.

▲ Director Yu's Talk: The reporter asked Yu Yan, who had only been in office for two months, about the many innovations in railway business that he had made, and the various aspects he had promoted, which were related to the country's century-long plan and were clearly visible to everyone. He was asked whether there would be any obstacles to promoting it in the future, and whether the national railways could be revived. As cargo transportation responsibility is the most fundamental policy of reform, the reporter raised several questions that the world may not fully understand and asked for detailed explanations. Director Yu answered as follows: (Question) Responsible transportation has been practiced in Europe and the United States for a long time, but it is still a new concept in China. Has anyone suggested it before? (Answer) The transportation conference in the eleventh year of the Republic passed a responsible transportation plan, but only a general rule was promulgated, and for ten years, except for the new railways in the Northeast, almost no railway has implemented it. (Question) Then why can it be resolutely implemented this time? (Answer) I have always been pragmatic in my work. If I can do one point, I will do it. This time, it is because the cargo transportation of each road has been declining day by day over the years, with all kinds of malpractices. Merchants have been exploited layer by layer and are suffering immensely. The future of the national economy is unthinkable. In order to complete the mission that the railway should bear, to relieve the suffering of merchants, and to develop the economy of the country and society, there is no other way but to implement responsible cargo transportation. Furthermore, in view of the repeated empty promises of responsible transportation that have not been implemented, this time I have hired experts to organize a committee to properly draft regulations, striving for perfection, so that there will be no obstacles after implementation. (Question) What are the current transportation methods and the measures of the transshipment companies? (Answer) The current malpractices are too numerous to mention. Merchants who transport goods, in addition to openly buying cargo cars, have to pay the so-called station fee. If this station fee is not paid, the station staff will deliberately create difficulties in the operation of the train, even to the point of not adding engine oil and causing the cargo cars to derail midway, and so on. A batch of goods may take months to be transported. Under this miserable situation, merchants have no choice but to pay more for transportation to the transshipment companies and ask them to send personnel to escort the goods. As a result, the transportation costs charged by the transshipment companies are several times higher than the railway's price. For example, on the Jinpu Railway, the railway transportation cost for one car of 10 tons of goods from Pukou to Xuzhou is 88 yuan, but when handled by a transshipment company, it costs 135 yuan. What crime have the merchants committed that they have to pay this extra handling fee? Merchants with weaker capital regard railway transportation as a daunting task, because the transportation costs are high, the costs are heavy, and sales are not easy. As a result, goods are congested in the place of origin and are unwilling to be transported out, and the economy of the national people is further depleted. (Question) Is there any certainty of implementing responsible transportation? (Answer) Of course there is certainty. Taking the Beijing-Ningbo Railway as an example, excluding the September 18th Incident last year, in just nine months, the income from the eleven stations that handled responsible transportation alone increased by 3.33 million. The preliminary trial run has been so effective that it can be done. If the whole country handles it uniformly, the hope for the future is truly limitless. (Question) Now that responsible transportation has been implemented, why is the freight rate increased by 10%? (Answer) The previous freight rate was set according to the transportation costs of each road and did not include the costs of responsible transportation. Now that responsible transportation has been implemented, the construction of cargo yards, the construction of warehouses, the purchase of tarpaulins, the increase of employees, the addition of cargo police, and other equipment that must be responsible, as well as compensation for losses, etc., will all be borne by the railway in the future. Therefore, the increase in costs is self-evident. (Question) How will the order of priority for transporting goods and the allocation of vehicles be handled in the future? (Answer) Goods will be transported on a first-come, first-served basis, and the allocation of vehicles will be absolutely open. If there are goods that need to be transported urgently, there are also priority and most-priority methods, but this is only a temporary measure in case the vehicles are not sufficient. In the future, when the vehicles are properly dispatched, there will be no backlog of goods in the warehouse, and they will be transported as soon as they arrive, so there will be no so-called priority and most-priority. (Question) What about the bill of lading? (Answer) The value of the bill of lading is equivalent to a valuable security. Merchants with a capital of 10,000 yuan can use it as collateral after a batch of goods is shipped and then load a second batch. Thus, the circulation is repeated, and 10,000 yuan can be used to make 30,000 to 40,000 yuan worth of transactions. This point is very important for the circulation of funds, and the railway can also help merchants make collateral. (Question) Now that responsible transportation has been implemented, it seems difficult for the railway to have a huge amount of funds to cover the compensation. (Answer) This level seems to be an over-concern. As a matter of fact, the railway will never allow merchants' goods to suffer losses. The Si-Tao Railway has an annual cargo transportation income of approximately 4 million yuan, and the average annual compensation is only over 7,000 yuan. Since the Beijing-Ningbo Railway began responsible transportation, the income for the whole year was 130 million yuan, and the compensation was only over 3,000 yuan. Therefore, the railway will strictly order its staff to work diligently, and compensation will not be a problem. (Question) Will the transshipment industry be affected in the future? (Answer) The railway absolutely has no intention of making things difficult for the transshipment companies, but it hopes that the transshipment companies will no longer wantonly exploit customers and purely adopt the principle of small profits and more transportation, so that their business will also be thriving. (Question) What if responsible transportation develops extremely rapidly and goods pile up like mountains, and the railway vehicles are insufficient? (Answer) According to current statistics, the vehicles on each road are delayed and wasted time, which is very uneconomical. The Ministry of Railways now stipulates a pattern. If cargo transportation develops, even four times more than in the past, there will be no shortage of vehicles. (Question) Are there any other obstacles after September 1st? (Answer) I ask myself, for the sake of the railway's future and to relieve the suffering of merchants, I resolutely organized it. There are absolutely no other thoughts mixed in. If anyone has high opinions, please teach me in writing at any time, and I will accept them as much as possible.

In my opinion, there should be no obstacles after implementation.

Yan Deqing Comes to Shanghai to Go to Europe 135

▲As Advisor to the Chinese Delegation to the League of Nations

The League of Nations conference is imminent. This conference will focus on the Northeast problem, and the railway issue is particularly important. Therefore, the Chinese delegation has specifically telegraphed Dr. Yan Deqing, Technical Advisor of the Ministry of Railways, to come and assist. Mr. Yan arrived in Shanghai the day before yesterday and has booked a cabin on an Italian mail ship sailing on September 5th to go directly to Geneva. Accompanying him is Mr. Guo Zouen Yuan, former member of the Northeast Communications Committee. Yan Yu Ji Yu, a native of Shanghai, is 53 years old. He graduated from Shanghai Yinghua Tongwen French School and graduated from Lehigh University in the United States with a Master of Engineering degree. After returning to China, he took the examination for returned students and was awarded the degree of Jinshi in engineering. He successively served as engineer of the Guangdong-Hankou and Shanghai-Nanjing Railways, chief engineer of the Beijing-Zhangjiakou Railway, deputy chief engineer of the Sichuan-Hankou Railway, technical advisor to the Shanghai Railway General Company, director of the Road Administration Department of the Nanjing Provisional Government, councilor and technical advisor of the Ministry of Communications, director of the Xiang-E Bureau of the Guangdong-Hankou Railway, Chinese representative of the technical department of the Allied Powers Joint Supervision of the Chinese Eastern and Siberian Railways, special commissioner of the Ministry of Communications to the United States, Britain, Belgium, and Germany to investigate railways, special member of the Chinese delegation to the Sino-Japanese Conference at the Pacific Conference, co-director of the Guangdong-Hankou and Sichuan-Hankou Railways, member of the Shandong Case Committee, attended the Sino-Japanese Conference, councilor of the Ministry of Railways, president of the Chinese Institute of Engineers, currently serving as technical advisor to the Ministry of Railways, director of the board of directors of the Sino-British Boxer Indemnity Committee, director of the Jiaoji Railway Council, president of the Chinese Engineering Society, and counselor of the Chinese representative office of the League of Nations Investigation Team. This time, he will serve as a special member of the Chinese delegation to the League of Nations Conference.

Shen Bao Fourth Sheet

Lawsuit Involving an Old Husband and a Young Concubine

▲Huzhou Girl Came to Shanghai to Avoid the Disaster of War

▲The Host's Warm Hospitality Led to Her Becoming a Concubine

▲Good Harmony for Eight Years Without Any Different Words

▲Sudden Discord Leads to a Lawsuit in Court

Zhu Lunqing, the owner of Yongju Money Shop in Ningbo Road, Tonghe Lane, is sixty-four years old. During the years when Qi Xieyuan and Lu Yongxiang were fighting in Jiangsu and Zhejiang, a fourteen-year-old Zhang girl from Huzhou came to Shanghai to avoid the disaster of war. Because she had some distant relationship with Zhu's concubine, Ms. Chen, she stayed at Zhu's house. Zhu saw that her face was quite beautiful, unlike a village girl, so even though the war had subsided, he insisted on keeping her. The girl also lost her parents when she was young, had few close relatives, and was alone. Returning home would leave her with no support and a difficult life. Fortunately, the host was hospitable, so she stayed with the thought of enjoying herself and forgetting her homeland. When she reached the age of fifteen or sixteen, Zhu used all kinds of teasing and paid special attention to her. Thereupon, the girl was defiled. Zhu's concubine then mediated and had Zhu take her as a concubine to avoid clandestine affairs and being laughed at by those who would catch them. The girl initially had no objection. After eight years, she had given birth to two sons and one daughter. Except for the eldest son who died young, the second son, Dahua, and the young daughter, Caifen, were all dearly loved by Zhu. Ms. Zhang was even more favored. Unexpectedly, Zhu's attitude has suddenly changed recently, and his treatment of Ms. Zhang is completely different from before, often abusing her. In the spring, he even wrote an agreement to sever the relationship, forcing her to sign it, wanting to implement a strategy of abandoning the box and keeping the pearl. However, Ms. Zhang was unwilling to sign, wanting to leave without a name, and it was difficult to live together. Therefore, she hired lawyer Jiang Yiping and filed a criminal lawsuit against Zhu in the First Special District District Court, recounting the circumstances of how she was deceived by Zhu when she was young, had a weak will, and lacked the ability to resist, and how she became Zhu's concubine after being seduced by Zhu's concubine, Ms. Chen. It was further stated that Zhu was old and confused, easily believed slander, and repeatedly abused her, making it difficult to maintain her life. However, she still lowered her head and humbled herself, hoping that he would wake up. Who knew that in March of this year, he suddenly forced her to sign a prepared agreement to sever the relationship. After begging, it was dropped. Moreover, the children born were still at the age of being cared for and raised, and the mother and children depended on each other for life and could not be separated even slightly. It was found that the defendant had committed the crime of raping a girl under the age of sixteen and abandoning a person without the ability to save herself, without providing the necessary support for her survival, which constituted a crime under Article 310, Paragraph 1 of the Criminal Law. It was requested that Zhu Lunqing be quickly ordered to be arrested and interrogated and severely punished according to law, and that all rights to incidental civil suits be reserved in order to warn against wickedness and maintain the rule of law. The court, according to the complaint, immediately issued a summons and sent a Chinese constable No. 1281, Jin Wanrong, to Yongju Money Shop yesterday to inform the defendant to appear in court for questioning on schedule. It is said that Zhu is already an old man, while the plaintiff, Zhu Zhang, is only in her twenties. When they appear in court on another day, the pear blossoms and begonias will be even more interesting.

Two National Goods Organizations Request Speedy Arbitration of Labor-Management Disputes 139

The Shanghai Citizens Promoting National Goods Association and the China National Goods Maintenance Association, in view of the tense situation of labor-management disputes in national goods factories and the tendency towards extremes, which is not conducive to the future of the national goods industry, telegraphed the Central Party Headquarters, the Executive Yuan, the Ministry of Industry, and the Municipal Party Headquarters and the Municipal Government yesterday, requesting them to investigate the facts and arbitrate as soon as possible. The original telegram reads: (Omitted titles) The promotion of national welfare and people's livelihood depends primarily on labor-management collaboration to develop production, resist the economic aggression of the foreign powers. Since September 18th, the social economy has suffered greatly. The Chinese goods factories have suffered tremendous losses in the Shanghai war. Due to financial constraints, they have all been forced to cut back. This is a common fact and is not desirable. Unfortunately, labor-management disputes have arisen and have been prolonged without resolution, creating a trend towards mutual destruction, making those who are determined to invest in revitalizing industry wary. Existing factories are in indescribable panic, only increasing the number of unemployed workers and leaving behind hidden worries for social security. The associations feel the danger and dare not remain silent. Therefore, they telegraphed your department and government, imploring you to consider the severity of the national crisis and the immaturity of industry, and to quickly telegraph the Shanghai authorities to promptly handle the labor-management disputes in national goods factories according to law, and earnestly investigate the facts and arbitrate as soon as possible. We await your orders with utmost urgency. Standing Committee Members of the Shanghai Citizens Promoting National Goods Association: Yu Hede, Feng Shaoshan, Chen Yiting, Chen Binghui, Fang Jiange, Xu Jianruo, Zhang Dezhai; Standing Committee Members of the China National Goods Maintenance Association: Wang Jie'an, Wang Hanqiang, Wang Xingyi; Respectfully requesting your investigation and decision, (sealed).

Repercussions of the Mass Movement Committee's Telegram Reaction 140

▲The Shanghai Publishing Industry Trade Union etc.The Shanghai Publishing Industry Trade Union and other organizations issued a statement regarding the labor dispute at the Sanyou Industrial Company, stating: Yesterday, we read in the newspapers that more than 40 factories, including Yixin Toothbrush Factory, made a statement regarding a telegram declaration from the Mass Movement Guidance Committee of the Central Party Headquarters, stating that yesterday, we read in the newspapers that regarding the labor-management dispute at the Shanghai Sanyou Industrial Company, the telegram from the Mass Movement Guidance Committee of the Central Party Headquarters to the Shanghai Municipal Party Headquarters and the Municipal Government stated that the telegram included phrases such as forcing the capitalist to resume work within a specified period of time by extraordinary means. According to Article 37 of the Provisional Constitution, people have the freedom to operate businesses. This is an absolute private right under the law. Forcing work to resume not only violates the spirit of the Provisional Constitution but also sets a bad precedent unseen in the world. China's industry is just emerging. For four or five years, the government has repeatedly issued orders and declarations to protect it. Now, the reality is the opposite, and the colleagues are even more fearful. Therefore, we dare to sincerely announce this, seeking the maintenance of public opinion and a legal and proper solution. The content of the statement obscures the facts and stubbornly quibbles, hoping to confuse the public and achieve their conspiracy to oppress workers. The Sanyou Industrial Company did not suffer significant losses in the recent Shanghai war and has no reason to suspend production. The truth of the matter has long been clarified by the central and municipal party and government agencies. However, the capitalist of the company is stubbornly cunning and uses this as an excuse to forcibly close the factory, causing more than a thousand workers to be displaced and unemployed, creating social panic. The workers of the company have repeatedly negotiated with the capitalist but have been rejected. Later, the Municipal Government and the Social Affairs Bureau mediated several times, but the capitalist firmly refused to accept, resulting in no resolution. After such delays for several months, there was no prospect of a solution. The workers of the company, seeing no hope for their livelihood, went on a hunger strike as a final plea, hoping that the capitalist would wake up and resume work quickly. However, the capitalist turned a blind eye to the fact that the workers had been on a hunger strike for several days and their lives were in danger, and did not move at all. People from all walks of life felt pity and resentment for the attitudes of both labor and capital. The Central Mass Movement Guidance Committee, also aware of the extraordinary period when the lives of the workers were in danger, issued an order to deal with the capitalist by extraordinary means. This policy, for the sake of fair treatment for both labor and capital, and for the sake of humanitarian justice, should be issued. As for the national law, it is intended to protect all the people, not just to guarantee the capitalists of the aristocratic class. The operation of the capitalist should be protected by law, but the livelihood of the workers is also protected by law. Moreover, factories are not allowed to suspend production freely. This is also clearly stated in the Constitution. These factories disregard the suffering of our workers and speak entirely from the standpoint of private interests, which further shows the viciousness of the capitalists. Moreover, they openly oppose the reasonable measures of the central authorities of the Party, which may have other intentions. The associations feel injustice at this preposterous argument and therefore make this correction, and request the central government to implement extraordinary measures to save the endangered lives of the Sanyou Company workers. Furthermore, the recent wave of labor unrest is entirely due to the illegal oppression of workers by the capitalists. Now, these factories have jointly issued a declaration, which shows a tendency to jointly oppress our workers. In the future, the status of our workers will inevitably become darker. Therefore, in order to protect the interests of our workers, it is even more necessary to unite and make a legitimate resistance. We hope that all the workers in the city will work together, and we hope that people from all walks of life will provide strong assistance, which will not only be the blessing of all the workers in the city but also the good fortune of the Party and the country. The Shanghai Publishing Industry Industrial Trade Union Reorganization Committee, the Shanghai Press Trade Union, the Shanghai First District Water and Electricity Industry Industrial Trade Union, the Seamen's Trade Union Maintenance Association, the Stevedores' Trade Union Two-Eight System Implementation Committee, the Shanghai East District Yarn Factory Trade Union Federation, the Shanghai Knitting Industry Trade Union, the Shanghai Sixth District Cigarette Industry Trade Union, the Shanghai Eighth District Cotton Spinning Industry Trade Union, the Shanghai Fifth District Loading and Unloading Trade Union, the Shanghai Fifth District Paper Industry Trade Union, the Shanghai Sixth District Lighterage Trade Union, the Shanghai Garment Industry Occupational Trade Union, the Shanghai Dongjiadu Ferry Trade Union, the Shanghai First District Knitting Industry Trade Union, the Shanghai Timber Transport Trade Union, the Shanghai Plywood Industry Industrial Trade Union, and other 27 trade unions jointly declare.

▲Declaration of Assistance from the Press Trade Union The Press Trade Union declared its support for the laid-off workers of the Sanyou Industrial Company, stating: It has been eight months since the Sanyou Industrial Company's labor unrest occurred, and it has not yet been resolved. It is not that the unity of our workers is not strong, but that the capitalists are deliberately trying to put the workers to death. Although the workers organized a hunger strike group to promote the capitalists' pity, the deranged capitalists turned a deaf ear and did not change their minds even slightly due to the hunger strike. Alas, how vicious! If they could wholeheartedly improve the factory's industry and develop domestic goods, so that money would not flow out, at a time when China is advocating domestic goods, Sanyou Industrial Company can be called the most developed industrial factory in China. Now, they want to put the workers to death and shut down the developing general factory. We recall that the Sanyou Industrial Company once had only a few hundred yuan in capital, and then gradually expanded to its current development. It is truly the crystallization of the sweat and blood of all the workers. The workers do their best to produce with the capitalists, and they also want the business to develop and the domestic products to be excellent. The workers are also concerned that foreign goods are increasingly flooding the market and domestic goods will be eliminated, so they strive for excellence and compete with foreign goods. Looking at the various products of Sanyou Industrial Company, compared with foreign goods, there is not much difference, and the goods produced are even better than imported goods, all created by the energy of the workers. Given these two points, now the Sanyou capitalists are repaying kindness with hatred, disregarding the livelihood of the workers, and wanting to achieve their goal of oppressing the workers. The Municipal Government, the Social Affairs Bureau, and the Municipal Party Headquarters have repeatedly mediated but have ignored them. They want to create social unrest. During this time of internal and external troubles, even genuinely loss-making industrial factories are still maintaining the livelihoods of the workers, let alone profitable factories. Now, the central government has sent personnel to Shanghai to investigate and force the Sanyou Industrial Company to restore its former state in order to maintain the livelihoods of the workers, but the Sanyou Industrial Company has rejected the order and contacted major industrial factories in China to publish declarations in various newspapers, implementing their great capital alliance and striving to create social panic, talking about Article 37 of the Provisional Constitution, which states that people have the freedom to operate businesses and that it is an absolute private right under the law. Moreover, we are under the economic oppression of foreign powers and suffering from the tragedy of natural and man-made disasters. Maintaining the status quo is already extremely difficult. We thought the capitalists did not know the various sufferings, but it turns out they do. You also know about natural and man-made disasters, so why do you do all kinds of vicious things? The workers have already suffered from natural and man-made disasters and are now suffering from the oppression of the capitalists. In Shanghai, where the cost of living is high, they can only barely make ends meet when they have a job. Once they suffer the pain of unemployment, how tragic will it be? Where is the capitalists' conscience? Moreover, Sanyou Company has always advocated domestic goods and treated workers well, so its business has gradually developed and has truly become the leader in the country. Last year, all factories were affected by the war, but Sanyou Company's business was better than in previous years because the people were driven by patriotism and bought domestic goods from Sanyou Industrial Company, so the profits were more than 300,000 yuan. The China Industrial Federation listened to Sanyou Company's one-sided story and echoed it, earning the notoriety of oppressing workers. Under the clear sky and bright sun, how can the people willingly accept the oppression of the capitalists? The workers follow Dr. Sun Yat-Sen's teachings and still embrace the spirit of labor-capital cooperation, and do not take any excessive actions, but wait quietly for the arbitration of the party and government agencies. However, the China Industrial Federation dares to destroy Dr. Sun Yat-Sen's teachings on protecting labor organizations, creating criminals who darken society. The colleagues of our association stand on the same position as the workers, our friendship is as deep as those in the same boat, and we are ready to go to life and death together. We are willing to fight with the capitalists, rather be a broken jade than an intact tile. All my workers, rise up together and fight to the death with the capitalists who are destroying the workers! Our association will lead more than a thousand workers to provide strong assistance. We hereby declare.

▲Trade Union Federation etc.The Trade Union Federation's declaration regarding the declaration of various factories and companies states: Yesterday, we read in the newspapers the declarations of dozens of factories, including Shanghai Yixin Toothbrush Factory, and the telegrams from the China Industrial Federation to the Central Party Headquarters and various ministries, which caused us great surprise. The labor-management dispute at the Sanyou Industrial Company has been through the local highest party headquarters together with the government to persuade the capitalists to quickly resume work in order to avoid the expansion of the dispute, but the capitalists disregarded the intentions of the party and government agencies and repeatedly delayed, causing the dispute to spread and the conflict to intensify. The well-intentioned mediation of the party and government agencies could not be realized. The workers were on a hunger strike and their lives were in danger, so the central government issued an order for mandatory enforcement to help them in their plight. Moreover, the Factory Law clearly stipulates that the suspension of a factory must first be approved by the government. The factory did not obtain the government's approval beforehand, but suddenly suspended operations. After the dispute occurred, it further violated the orders of the party and government agencies and refused to resolve it, resorting to vicious means such as cutting off workers' food and stopping water supply to suppress the workers. Its illegal and unreasonable actions have long been despised by public opinion. Freedom of business is indeed enshrined in the Provisional Constitution, but freedom is only possible within the scope of the law. Suspension of business without notifying the government means that there is no freedom to speak of. All my workers should unanimously demand that the central government resolutely implement mandatory measures to warn against cunning and maintain social order. Moreover, the telegram from the China Industrial Federation contains the words "sacrificing the existing" and "throwing" everything away. Such obvious threats and unified walls are attacking us workers. If we workers do not seek a way to survive, then the workers will die of starvation, jump into the river and die, but cannot move the hearts of the capitalists who eat fat meat and cook thick food, and the central government's orders cannot be carried out by the group of wealthy people who own assets and live in mansions. Are we workers still human? Fellow workers, the situation is urgent, and the matter is dangerous. Rather than enduring grievances, allowing others to cut us into pieces, sell us off piecemeal, and die, why not rise up together, support the central government in implementing mandatory orders, and not stop until the goal is achieved? Let us encourage each other. We hereby declare, members of the Shanghai Trade Union Federation, the Newspaper Delivery Occupational Trade Union, the Cantonese Steamboat Wood Industry Weaving Industry Trade Union, the Fourth District Silk Reeling Industry Industrial Trade Union, the Ink Manufacturing Occupational Trade Union, the Municipal Tea Industry Workers Trade Union, the Municipal Cured Meat Industry Occupational Trade Union, the Municipal Leather Manufacturing Industry Industrial Trade Union, the Municipal Piano Industry Industrial Trade Union, the Municipal Third District Coal Silk Reeling Industry Industrial Trade Union, the Sixth District Silk Reeling Industry Industrial Trade Union, the Municipal Civilian Shipbuilding Wood Industry Occupational Trade Union, the Fifth District Water Wood Industry Trade Union, the Municipal Card Industry Trade Union, the Municipal Lithographic Printing Industry Industrial Trade Union, the Municipal Umbrella Industry Trade Union, the Second District Pier Trade Union, the Fourth District Pier Trade Union, the Fifth District Garment Industry Trade Union, the Municipal Winery Occupational Trade Union, the Municipal Jar Repair Industry Occupational Trade Union, the Duck Slaughtering Industry Occupational Trade Union, the First District Pier Trade Union, the Municipal New Taikoo Wharf Workers Trade Union, etc., 34 trade unions jointly declare.

After the Workers of Sanyou Factory Resumed Eating 141

▲Still Hospitalized for Treatment

▲Talks on the Factory Fire

Hong Jiaben and others, the workers of the Sanyou Industrial Cooperative General Factory in Yinxiang Port who went on a hunger strike, have shown signs of improvement in their spirits since resuming eating on the evening of the 25th, but they are still hospitalized. Yesterday, the person in charge of the union gave a speech on the factory fire. The details are as follows:

▲Hunger Strike Workers Still in Hospital. After thirty-one workers including Hong Jiaben voluntarily went on a hunger strike, Party and government agencies repeatedly sent personnel to persuade them to eat, but to no avail. Subsequently, the Party and government agencies issued a joint notice from the Municipal Party Department and the Social Affairs Bureau, stating that the municipal government had decided to formally arbitrate the case on the 31st, and a solution was not far off, urging them to resume eating to avoid accidents. The workers complied and announced their resumption of eating that evening. Yesterday morning, the 7th District Cotton Weaving Industry Union sent two directors, Gong Yuting and Bao Boyi, to the Labor Hospital and Shanghai Hospital to visit and express their condolences. They saw that the workers' spirits had reached a good state, but many suffered from headaches and foot pain, and had not yet fully recovered. Therefore, they are still hospitalized for treatment. ▲Labor Committee Speaks on Factory Fire. The Standing Director of the 7th District Cotton Weaving Industry Union gave a speech on the factory fire that occurred the day before yesterday (the 27th), saying, "When the factory fire occurred the other day, the workers discovered it and immediately requested to enter the first half to inspect whether the fire started inside the factory. Unexpectedly, they were stopped by the police force. The reason for this is difficult to understand. After negotiations, they were allowed to enter and put out the fire. At this time, the Yangshupu Fire Brigade also drove to the scene, and the fire was extinguished in about twenty minutes. After much investigation, no leads were found. Since the workers entered the factory on June 2nd, until the police brigade stationed on the 21st of this month, strict precautions were taken, and no disasters occurred. Later, with the police brigade stationed in the factory for protection, there was no concern for accidents. Unexpectedly, on the night of the 17th, a fire suddenly broke out in the factory buildings along Ma Yushan Road, and now there is another fire alarm in broad daylight. At a time when this dispute has not been resolved, such an unfortunate event has occurred. It is clear that villains are sabotaging from within, trying to harm the workers. Therefore, in order to clarify the truth, this union must ask the Party and government agencies to thoroughly investigate."

British Public Bus Strike News Yesterday 142

The strike at the British Public Bus Company has been going on for twenty days and has not yet been resolved. The detained workers have not yet been released. The strike committee has hired pro bono lawyers to prepare for court defense. The details are as follows:

▲Strike Committee Statement. The strike committee, fearing misunderstandings from the outside world due to recent incidents of vehicle damage, injuries, and other unfortunate events, issued a statement yesterday saying, "Workers have endured a painful strike due to the devastation and oppression of imperialist capitalists. The company has intensified its efforts to forcibly resume operations, making it impossible for workers to maintain their livelihoods. This committee will abide by the wishes of all workers, maintain order, and await mediation from Party and government agencies and legal entities. This committee has not been involved in the recent disturbances outside. We fear misunderstandings from the outside world, so we hereby declare."

▲Hiring Lawyers. Ticket sellers No. 199 and No. 124 were arrested by the police and interrogated by the court. They are still detained. The workers are outraged and have decided to go to court to petition for their release when the trial begins. They have also hired lawyer Li Aokui to defend them in court.

▲Petition Today. All the workers decided at a meeting the day before yesterday to petition the municipal government yesterday. Therefore, all the workers planned to depart yesterday. However, because yesterday was Sunday, a regular holiday for the municipal government, they decided to change it to this morning to petition and request a prompt mediation to resolve the issue as soon as possible.

▲New Workers and Security. Since the outbreak of the strike, the company has hired more than one hundred new workers to maintain operations and assigned them to various vehicles. Recently, due to disturbances, many new workers have been injured. Yesterday, the company issued each new worker a police whistle for security purposes, in case of need.

Reward for the Arrest of the Main Culprit in the Arson of the Updated Stage 147

The Shanghai Public Security Bureau issued a notice yesterday, which reads, "Notice of Reward: According to a report submitted by merchant Gu Zhuxuan and others, Zhuxuan, in order to revitalize the market after the Japanese invasion of Zhabei, entered into a lease agreement with the owner of the Updated Stage at No. 6 Menggu Road and took over the operation of the Updated Stage, spending a lot of money on repairs and decorations. We have already submitted a detailed report requesting your approval for the arrest. Zhuxuan and the owner of the building have jointly raised 5,000 yuan each, totaling 10,000 yuan, and deposited it in Zhejiang Bank as a reward for the personnel involved in purchasing leads and making arrests. It is assumed that the mastermind and the arsonists burned this public entertainment stage to revitalize the market. Their intentions must be to harm society and disrupt order. It is definitely not a simple act against an entertainment stage that has no grievances with anyone. Their other intentions and the organization of the bandits are obvious. If we do not promptly publish a reward notice for their arrest and conduct strict investigations, it will not be enough to maintain local peace. Therefore, arson is a matter that requires strict arrest and punishment. In addition to issuing orders to all subordinates to investigate and arrest, we hereby issue a notice to inform the public. If the main culprit is found, a reward of 10,000 yuan will be given as an encouragement. This is hereby announced."

Shanghai Supplement of the Shen Bao

Statements

Abolition and Prevention 155

— Buddha

The meaning of the two characters "abolition" is to abolish and stop. However, it does not make clear whether it is self-abolition or abolition by others. But the meaning of the two characters "prevention" is different, meaning that there is mandatory enforcement. Even if the authorities are unwilling to stop, one still wants to enforce it strongly. Therefore, the meanings of the two characters "abolition" and "prevention" are quite different.

Yesterday, the Great League for the Abolition of Civil War was held in Shanghai, with 449 representatives from various provinces and cities. It can be said to be an unprecedented grand gathering. One member proposed that the two characters "abolition" should be changed to "prevention", which is indeed more meaningful. Because calling for peace and stopping civil war has been going on for many times in the past 20 years. However, the warlords, while signing peace agreements, still opened the door wide and fought their battles. What is the meaning of such appeals? What is the effect of such agreements?

Therefore, a member advocated that the two characters "abolition" should be changed to "prevention", to change from a request-style to a mandatory-style. This is indeed very valuable. However, the guns are in their hands. What methods do you have to prevent it? How much ability do you have to prevent it? As in the proposal, there are also methods to prevent civil war. The general method is non-cooperation. May I ask, in previous civil wars, which one was cooperated and approved by the people? It can be seen that the effectiveness of the proposed method is also equal to zero.

However, the definition of the so-called "civil war" is even more difficult to say. For example, the suppression of the Communists, is it a civil war, or is it not a civil war? If it is a civil war, then should the Communists be allowed to move around everywhere? If it is not a civil war, then it is actually in the form of a civil war. Moreover, on the one hand, imperialists shout loudly and implement their annexation policies, while on the other hand, communists harass everywhere. Even if we want to resist foreign aggression, we cannot unite our forces. We will inevitably find excuses. Therefore, the Communist Party should also change its policy at this time and shout the slogan of uniting against foreign aggression.

To put it more thoroughly, this is not the time to shout for the abolition of civil war. It is the time to shout for unity and joint resistance to foreign aggression. If we only talk about the abolition of civil war, like the northern generals' advocacy of non-resistance, in a few days, they completely presented the 30 million people and tens of millions of square miles of land outside the customs. At that time, there was no so-called civil war in the north. In this way, although there is no civil war, it is no different from civil war. Therefore, what should be discussed now is how to thoroughly resist foreign aggression and how to recover lost territories, which is the best strategy.
