Science

Method of Manufacturing Agar-agar 158

— Slave

Since the September 18th Incident, the Chinese people have once again chanted the slogan of boycotting enemy goods and breaking off economic relations, because the scars suffered this time are relatively deep, so its temporality will not be five minutes. "Remembering the past is a guide for the future." Since we know that the previous boycotts were temporary and passive, and often wasted a lot of precious energy after the event, without getting any price, we should now take a further step and make a permanent and active boycott, that is, for enemy goods that our country does not have substitutes for, study how to make them, and actively hurry up to make them. Compared with a monotonous passive boycott, the effect is more than ten times greater. Now, I will briefly write down the method of manufacturing agar-agar in enemy goods below.

In July and August, go to the coastal areas of our country to collect fresh Gracilaria (available in dried seafood stores), wash it with fresh water, soak it for three or four days, take it out and dry it in the sun. After drying, use ten catties of Gracilaria, soak it in a solution of nine taels of bleaching powder, two qian of sulfuric acid, and six sheng of clear water (this solution should be filtered first). After about ten minutes, when the vegetable turns white, take it out and soak it in lime milk. In less than three minutes, wash it in clear water, mash it with a stone pestle, and then bleach it with clear water to remove any other odors from the raw material, then put it in a pot, add five times the amount of water, and boil it. Add a little rice vinegar and stir gently while boiling. After about half an hour, change to a slow fire, and when the vegetable is completely dissolved, remove the fire, squeeze the juice with a cloth, put the obtained liquid juice back into the pot and boil it to reduce the water content. When it turns into a paste, pour it into a tree plate and wait for it to solidify (the temperature should be high at this time, otherwise it will not easily solidify). Then cut it into paste strips about one foot long and two inches wide with a knife, and then cut the thick strips into thin strips with a dividing machine, dry them in the sun, and they will become white agar-agar like silver threads.

Editor's note, I think agar-agar is widely used in our country, and it can indeed be manufactured according to this method. However, when it is about to solidify, do not cut it with a knife, but filter it out using the method of making vermicelli, or squeeze it out using a noodle-making machine. I wonder if it is possible? I respectfully ask Mr. Nu for his opinion.

Social Improvement Discussion Group

My Opinion on Improving Bathhouses 159

— I

Here, what I am talking about is not the exquisite bathrooms in high-rise buildings, but the bathhouses in the streets and alleys that are exclusively for the use of ordinary citizens. Let's start by saying a few words about the existing ones.

(1) Everyone knows that bathing has a great relationship with health. It can be said that if someone never bathes in their life, then they will have a reduced lifespan, or at least have a weakened body. This is because regular bathing can make the pores comfortable, so that the dirt in the body can be fully discharged. Therefore, bathing is an indispensable part of life for anyone, and it is by no means limited to a certain group of people. However, most poor people not only do not have complete bathing facilities, but also cannot afford to spend a few cents to go to a bathhouse once. Of course, some people cannot take a comfortable bath even once in the entire hot season, let alone in winter.

(2) As long as you have been to a bathhouse once, you will definitely feel that the water in the so-called "pool" is too unclean. A pool of hot water dyed grayish-white with body dirt is full of scabies patients. People with syphilis are scratching frantically. (As for the so-called private rooms, elegant seats, and special elegant seats, etc., of course, they are not within the scope of this article.) So spending a lot of money is just buying skin diseases back.

(3) In such a large Shanghai, there are only a few bathhouses. So if you are determined to take a bath, you have to spend a lot of tram fare. At the same time, because the fees for bathhouses are too high, each time costs at least five cents or more.

(4) It seems that it has been generally recognized that women do not need to bathe: otherwise, why are there so few bathhouses for women in this undeveloped Shanghai? I have limited knowledge and I am not a woman, so I only know that there are a few on Fourth Malu that seem to be opened for prostitutes (I have to repeat again, Turkish baths, bathing in hotels, ... are not within the scope of this article.)

(5) ... Of course there are more, but I can't remember them all at once.)

Looking at it this way, I have the following opinions on bathhouses.

(1) Opening bathhouses is one of the main social undertakings, that is, to enable everyone to have the opportunity to bathe often. And to make the habit of bathing universal to every citizen.

(2) All bathhouses should use pools, which should not be too large, so that water can be changed constantly, and at the same time, it will not consume too much hot water. Everyone can only use soap to wash themselves as clean as possible outside the pool, and use a basin to scoop water to wash themselves clean, and then immerse themselves in the pool, so that the pool water will not be easily contaminated.

(3) People with skin diseases are absolutely prohibited from entering, so as to avoid infection.

(4) Bathhouses should not charge too high fees, at most one cent. And crack down on all extra expenses. Because bathhouses do not need to be overly extravagant, just one stove, one pool, and one sitting room can do the trick, which can greatly save capital: even if the income is small, it can be supported. What's more, gradually develop the habit of people bathing every day, and at the same time, people have the economic possibility of bathing every day: of course, there will be many customers, and business will naturally be booming.

(5) Women's bathhouses can be incorporated into general bathhouses, just set up another room, so that women can have equal enjoyment. (At the same time, children can also be treated equally)

(6) Bathhouses must be common, even one bathhouse on average for every hundred households. On a grander scale, it should be common in rural areas and common throughout the country.

(7) There's more, there's more.

Of course, the above methods, if it is a peaceful and prosperous age, the government has a major responsibility to promote it. However, now... alas!

This opinion is based on the facilities in Japan (even at this time of "national crisis", I hope that I will not be given the title of "pro-Japanese"?). Enthusiastic gentlemen, please visit the Japanese bathhouses in Hongkou.

This humble sincerity is respectfully presented to you, and I hope that you will teach me something.

Finally, I have to say: "Only with healthy citizens can there be a healthy country." Bathing can help promote health, which is of course cultivating the country's strength. I have added a few words to supplement the lack of the aforementioned reasons.

Sadness

Father and Son 160

— He

Now it's raining heavily again. I've closed all the windows around me. I'm heavily smoking a cigarette. I'm quietly listening to the sound of thunder and rain. I'm waiting for the lightning to flash in front of me again and again.

So my mood is both troubled and peaceful, so I recall a story from nine years ago.

It was also a rainy day like this. At that time, my friend Wang and I were closed in the house, letting the rain and wind blow outside the window. But Wang told me about his childhood. 丨The following is his narration.

"You know, the most miserable child is the one who loses his mother in childhood. This may not be something that everyone has experienced, but I have deeply tasted this kind of suffering.

I grew up in a poor peasant family. Of course, in such a simple family of a poor peasant, the death of my mother was undoubtedly a major blow to my father. Poor father had to get me up early, cook breakfast for himself, and then teach me to carry lunch with him to the fields. He told me stories while working. When he was tired, he taught me to sleep under the shade of a tree, letting ants and flies play on me. When the north wind blew, I had to curl up in my clothes and cry. The morning was like this, and so was after lunch. Until dusk, I rode home on the back of a cow.

My parents loved each other very much. This can be seen from my father's narration. I am my mother's only son, and also my father's only son. It is precisely because of my mother's death that I feel the greatness of my father's benevolence. I can get full proof of this.

Once, I was beaten and bled by the child next door. Of course, I had to endure it, because I always wanted to find an opportunity to retaliate once. One evening, I actually found this opportunity. I beat his nose until it bled the same way, so I won. But soon the child cried and led his mother to my house. At that time, my father was washing his feet. I only heard the woman pointing at my father and saying:

"Your child is too hateful. You must teach him a lesson. Look, he beat my child until he bled."

"Dad!" I snatched and retorted: "He beat me and bled last time, but I didn't tell you like him."

So my father comforted the child's mother, apologized carefully, and shouted at me, I cried. So the child walked away triumphantly. But I was insulted, I was very sad. Soon I watched my father turn his face and say to me in a low voice:

"Child, I didn't beat you, why are you still crying? You have to know that you shouldn't quarrel with them, you can only suffer, because you are a child without a mother!"

So my father also sobbed.

But he didn't spoil me that much.

Once, I ran back from a private school, and tried my best to cover it up in front of my father. Father didn't say a word, I felt very relieved. At dinner, he especially reminded me and said:

"You eat more rice tonight."

"Why?" I asked:

"For no reason."

After dinner, my father sat in the lawn. As usual, I approached him, but he grabbed me with one hand, and picked up his shoe and hit me on the back, shouting:

"Will you skip school next time?"

"Dad!" I cried: "No, I dare not anymore."

This lesson was very effective for me, and since then I have developed the habit of studying hard. Perhaps this kind of internal punishment was my father's best teaching method."

Mr. Wang stopped talking. But he was still silent in his memories. After that, I asked him and said:

"Then you finally didn't have a stepmother?"

"This may be for my sake."

The number of days detained before the judgment is finalized will be converted to imprisonment at a rate of two days of detention for one day of imprisonment. One package of opium paste, weighing thirty-six taels, is confiscated.

Judgment on Chai Ming's Opium Case (Main Text): 180

Chai Ming-kui is sentenced to six months of imprisonment with a fine of $150 for possessing opium with the intent to sell. If the fine is not fully paid after compulsory execution, it will be commuted to imprisonment at a rate of one dollar for one day. The number of days detained before the judgment is finalized will be converted to imprisonment at a rate of two days of detention for one day of imprisonment. Eighteen taels of opium are confiscated. A Judgment Regarding the Lawsuit Between Wen Da-nian and Yan Song-zhou and Others Due to Borrowing Money (Main Text): 194

The defendants Yan Song-zhou and Jin Quan-fu shall jointly repay the plaintiff $750, with the lawsuit costs borne equally by the defendants. This notice is specifically for the defendant Yan Song-zhou's information.

A Judgment Regarding the Lawsuit Between Zhu Lin-sheng and Zhou Zhi-kun Due to Debt (Main Text): 195

The defendant shall pay the plaintiff silver $500, with an annual interest rate of 2% from April 12th, 1931, until the day of execution. The plaintiff's remaining claims are dismissed. The lawsuit costs shall be borne by the defendant.

A Judgment Regarding the Lawsuit Between Fumei Company and Xia Gui-xing and Others Due to Rent (Main Text): 196

The defendant Xia Gui-qing shall pay the plaintiff $46.50. Cai Shou-jian shall pay the plaintiff $92.50. Lu Zhi-lan shall pay the plaintiff $47.50. Zhou Ting-xun shall pay the plaintiff $60.06. If Xia Gui-xing is unable to pay, the defendant Tailong Company shall be jointly responsible for $44 of the debt. The plaintiff's remaining claims and request for provisional execution are dismissed. The plaintiff shall bear 9/14 of the lawsuit costs, excluding the costs of the provisional execution request and the withdrawn portion. The defendant Cai Shou-jian shall bear 2/14, and Xia Gui-xing, Lu Zhi-lan, and Zhou Ting-xun shall each bear 1/14. (Above are from August 25th)
